# Hive Mind — Session Log (Append-Only)

### 2026-05-12 night → 2026-05-13 early-hours (~6h) — D:/ECOSIRE.COM — Marketplace Phase 1 COMPLETION (flag still OFF, 515/618 cells live, 222 repos auto-syncing)
- **9 commits across 5 prod-deploy rounds** on `ecosire/ecosire.com` (HEAD = `9c639880`). Resumed from 2026-05-12 Phase 1 deploy where flag stayed OFF because AWS S3 + IAM creds were never set up and product_files was 0 rows. This session built the foundation end-to-end.
- **New AWS infra**: S3 bucket `ecosire-apps` (us-east-1, Block Public Access on all 4, versioning enabled, SSE-S3) + IAM user `ecosire-marketplace` + min-privilege policy `ecosire-apps-s3` + access key installed on prod `/opt/ecosire/app/.env.local`. Bucket name chosen `ecosire-apps` (not legacy `ecosire-products`) for SEO + alignment with Odoo's `apps.odoo.com` nomenclature.
- **New shared secret `ECOSIRE_SYNC_TOKEN`** (64-char hex) — installed on prod env + as github.com/ecosire org-level secret (visibility=all). Powers the new webhook auth path. Token VALUE in 2 places only (prod .env.local + GitHub org secret); reference-only here.
- **New marketplace webhook** `POST /api/internal/github-sync` at `apps/api/src/modules/github-sync/` — Bearer-auth via `crypto.timingSafeEqual`, rate-limited 30/min, CSRF-exempt (BOTH `/api/` and non-prefixed forms), idempotent via deterministic-archiver sha8 collision check, full audit trail to `module_build_logs`. CRSF middleware exemption pattern is now documented as standalone feedback memo for any future @Public() POST endpoint.
- **GitHub Actions fleet install — 222 of 222 ecosire/* repos** got `.github/workflows/sync-to-s3.yml` via `scripts/install-github-action-sync.sh`. Future tag pushes (`v17.0.x.x.x` / `v18.0.x.x.x` / `v19.0.x.x.x`) anywhere in the org now auto-fire the webhook → S3 PUT + product_files INSERT. **This changes the steady-state workflow for every D:/Development module-developer agent** — no more manual backfill after `publish_all_modules_v3.py`, the marketplace catches up itself.
- **License-version download gate (security)**: `apps/api/src/modules/downloads/downloads.service.ts:getDownloadUrl` now enforces `license.odooVersion === file.odooVersion` (normalized via `normalizeOdooMajor`). Closes a real pre-existing gap where a v17-license holder who knew a v19 fileId could pull a pre-signed URL. 3 new vitest cases cover it. `verifyEntitlement` also tightened to filter `isNull(deletedAt)` for defense in depth.
- **Schema-drift repair** on prod: `ALTER TABLE product_files ADD COLUMN organization_id text NOT NULL REFERENCES organizations(id)` + `idx_product_files_org`; same on `download_logs`. Drizzle code declared these columns long ago but `packages/db/src/migrate.ts` wrong-folder bug ([[Pattern - Drizzle migrate.ts wrong path]]) meant they never landed on prod. Tables were empty so ALTER NOT NULL was safe.
- **DB hygiene**: 6 of Amir's own test licenses (engr.mohammadamirnazir@gmail.com) soft-deleted via `status='revoked' + deleted_at + deleted_reason` + 1 inconsistent row (deleted_at set but status='active' since 2026-04-18) reconciled. Backup at prod `/tmp/licenses-backup-20260512-181410.jsonl`. Remaining 5 real-customer licenses: Bimal × 2 (Daraz v17+v18 explicit), Quicken/wayfair, Ziad/shopify, Tariq/trendyol (last 3 still NULL `odoo_version` — awaiting customer claim).
- **17 product `metadata.odooTechnicalName` overrides** applied (slug→technical-name derivation guessed wrong on many): `mercado-libre`→`mercadolibre`, `11street`→`elevenstreet`, `pinterest-shopping`→`pinterest`, `whatsapp-business`→`whatsapp`, `youtube-shopping`→`youtube`, `facebook-meta-shop`→`facebook`, `instagram-shopping`→`instagram`, `xiaohongshu-red`→`xiaohongshu`, `kakao-commerce`+`kakaotalk-shopping`→`kakao` (storefront duplicate flagged), `zozotown`→`zozo`, `kaspi-kz`→`kaspi`, `finn-no`→`finn`, `dewu-poizon`→`dewu`, `douyin-shop`→`douyin`, `line-shopping`→`line`, `naver-shopping`→`naver`, `snapchat-shopping`→`snapchat`. New scripts: `wire-modules-from-github.cjs`, `resolve-unwired-products.cjs`, `final-gap-audit.cjs`.
- **Final marketplace coverage**: 515 product_files rows (was 0), 519 active module_registry rows (was 414), 515 S3 objects under `apps/`. **164 / 206 products fully covered (80%)**. Flag `MODULES_MARKETPLACE_V1` stays **OFF** until 42 remaining coverage gaps close — user decision: NO product disable (keep all 206 visible on storefront for SEO + customer-acquisition). Complete dev-handoff doc at `D:/ECOSIRE.COM/_reports/HANDOFF-2026-05-13-marketplace-gaps.md` lists every gap by category (20 partial needing v17+v19 publish, 2 needing v17+v18 (incl URGENT wildberries before 2026-06-23 sunset), 1 needing first-ever tags (elevenstreet), 1 storefront duplicate decision, 20 needing build).
- **5 fleet-affecting feedback memos captured** for cross-workspace use: (1) `feedback_archiver_deterministic_zip` — archiver embeds `new Date()` per entry breaking sha-based idempotency; always pass `{date: new Date(0)}`; (2) `feedback_drizzle_defaultfn_raw_sql` — Drizzle `$defaultFn(() => crypto.randomUUID())` only fires through ORM; raw `postgres-js` SQL bypasses → INSERT fails with null-id constraint; always supply UUIDs explicitly in .cjs scripts; (3) `feedback_gh_cli_windows_quirks` — three reproducible Windows git-bash issues (gh api leading-slash → filesystem path; gh repo list GraphQL 400; gh auth status keyring race) + jq not installed → use python; (4) `feedback_schema_drift_organization_id` — Drizzle .notNull() without DB-level default + missing migration = silent until first INSERT; documents 9 known still-unrepaired drifts plus the repair pattern; (5) `feedback_csrf_exempt_per_endpoint` — checklist for every new @Public() POST endpoint (both path forms in exemptPaths + ALLOWED_PUBLIC_ENDPOINTS spec + smoke-test pattern).
- Cross-project impact: **HUGE — the GitHub Action workflow in 222 ecosire/* repos changes the steady-state flow for every D:/Development module pump**. Any module-developer agent that pushes a new `v{N}.0.x.x.x` tag will now auto-publish a downloadable ZIP to the storefront within ~5 seconds of the push. This eliminates manual `wire-missing-modules-to-registry.cjs` + backfill steps from the publishing skill. Also: the 5 fleet feedback memos apply to every NestJS workspace (`Drizzle $defaultFn`, `archiver determinism`, `gh CLI Windows quirks`, `CSRF exempt-per-endpoint`) — promoted as workspace memories for now, ready to graduate to Unity `04 - Resources/Patterns/` on second occurrence.

- **4 fleet-affecting lessons captured**: (1) `feedback_vitest_decorator_metadata.md` — vitest+esbuild does NOT emit TS decorator metadata; NestJS DI silently passes `undefined` for controller constructor params compiled at test runtime; workaround = explicit `@Inject(Service)` on controllers in apps/api/src/ exercised by real-DB integration tests; pre-built packages (@ecosire/auth-core) work because tsc emits the metadata into dist/. **Applies to ANY NestJS workspace.** (2) `feedback_migrate_ts_wrong_path.md` — one-line fix in next session: `'migrations'` → `'drizzle'` in migrate.ts + remove `|| true` from deploy Step 8. (3) `feedback_nodemailer_subpath_leak.md` — `@ecosire/utils` top-level re-export of server-only `NodemailerMailerAdapter` dragged nodemailer + 13 Node builtins into apps/web client bundle; fix is subpath `@ecosire/utils/mailer` + stub files for moduleResolution:node compat. (4) Test-env schema drift extends to `support_tickets` + `support_ticket_replies` + 2 enums (not just `user_role` enum from 2026-04-23) — test-helper `applyPreMigrationDrift` now CREATEs all four; permanent fix would be a new migration `0010_schema_drift_repair.sql`.
- Pre-existing prod state surprises: 0 of 215 products had `prod-` slug prefix (CLAUDE.md memory said ~158 — was outdated). Slug rename runner was a no-op. The 301 redirect logic in proxy.ts stays as defence-in-depth.
- Cross-project impact: **vitest+esbuild decorator-metadata gap applies to every workspace running NestJS integration tests with vitest** (D:/ECOSIRE.AI's FastAPI is unaffected; D:/ECOSIRE.IO doesn't use NestJS heavily yet; future NestJS workspaces should default to explicit `@Inject` to avoid this trap).
- Canonical facts promoted to Unity: [[Reference - vitest NestJS decorator metadata gap]] (new — applies cross-workspace).

### 2026-05-12 evening (~3h continuous + autonomous-loop wakeups) — D:/Development — TWO v19 RNG strictness regressions identified + fixed fleet-wide; OWL fleet swept clean
- **Regression 1 — `<group expand=/string=>` inside `<search>` view**: 35 modules affected, all fixed + published. Demo install of googleshopping confirmed v19 `<rng:define name="group">` removed both attributes; cascading lxml error "search has extra content: field" misattributed the cause until empirical demo install. ### 2026-05-10 late night → 2026-05-11 00:30 — D:/Development — Bimal Daraz r5 (wizard view validator + v17 JS rpc backport) + v17 source disaster recovery from gutted state + Playwright walk-through verified
- Bimal r4 install bounced on **wizard view validator** error: `Field 'status' used in modifier 'invisible' must be present in view but is missing`. Odoo 17/18/19 view validators require every field referenced by ANY modifier (`invisible=` / `readonly=` / `required=`) to be DECLARED somewhere in the view's ARCH tree, even invisibly — `status` was on the wizard models but never declared in the 4 wizard form views. Fixed by adding `<field name="status" invisible="1"/>` (plus `test_result` + `test_success` on connection wizard) directly under `<form>` in Import / Export / Mapping / Test Connection wizard view files. Shipped as `daraz_store_management 17.0.5.0.3`.
- **Caught + fixed v17-only JS backport miss while auditing**: `static/src/js/daraz_dashboard.js` imported `rpc` from `@web/core/network/rpc` — that path was introduced in Odoo 18. Odoo 17 still uses `@web/core/network/rpc_service` with `jsonrpc` export. The bad import silently fails in browser, the component never registers, and clicking Daraz Dashboard menu throws `KeyNotFoundError: Cannot find daraz_dashboard in this registry`. Fixed with `import { jsonrpc as rpc } from "@web/core/network/rpc_service";` aliased — rest of file unchanged. v18 + v19 don't need this change.
- **V17 SOURCE DISASTER RECOVERY**: discovered `D:/Development/odoo17/server/odoo/` was gutted by May 2 wipe (zero .py files left, only __pycache__). User provided `D:/Downloads/odoo_17.0+e.20260510.tar.gz` (346MB Community+Enterprise official build). Restored: gutted dir backed up at `server/odoo.gutted_2026_05_10/`, extracted tarball over the gap, created 4-line `server/odoo-bin` wrapper, used SYSTEM Python (`C:/Users/Amir Nazir/AppData/Local/Programs/Python/Python312/python.exe`) NOT bundled (also broken — missing `Lib/encodings/`). Custom `addons/` (123 modules) UNTOUCHED throughout (verified pre + post extraction). NSSM service `odoo-server-17.0` had been auto-paused on May 2 23:40 due to source gap.
- **Full Playwright walk-through done before delivery** (user's explicit ask: "do complete installation and playwright testing yourself before providing update"). Installed v17.0.5.0.3 on fresh DB `daraz_v17_r5_test` → state=installed, 1,332 xmlids, 11 daraz form views. Started HTTP on :8070 with `--dev=assets`, cleared cookie + ir_attachment cache, walked all 4 wizards (Import, Export, Mapping, Test Connection) + Dashboard (6 KPI cards, 2 charts, Quick Actions) → all render with ZERO JS console errors. 5 verification PNG screenshots saved.
- **r5 delivery shipped to Bimal 2026-05-11 ~00:30**: `Bimal-Daraz-v17-v18-r5.zip` (2.76MB, 306 entries — both fixes verified inside zip via py inspection) + `EMAIL_TO_BIMAL_r5.md` + 5 verification screenshots. ### 2026-05-10 (morning) — D:/Development — Obliq + Oenoteca IAP unblock: NEW Cause 3 for `iap_extract` `KeyError: 'status'` (filesystem-vs-registry split brain on `private_enterprise`) + AP workflow runbook delivered
- User reported recurring `KeyError: 'status'` at 11:20 GMT on Obliq during click-to-digitize a vendor bill (`account.move._upload_to_extract` line 270 — UPLOAD path). Different code path than the polling cron the 2026-05-08 postmortem tested, which is why that postmortem had concluded "system already remediated". Cause 3 found: `private_enterprise` was registry-uninstalled on 2026-05-08 11:10 UTC but the addon directory was still on `/opt/odoo/instances/obliq/addons/` so every Odoo worker boot re-imported `__init__.py` and re-applied the monkey-patch on `iap.iap.iap_jsonrpc`. Smoking gun was a `WARNING odoo.addons.private_enterprise: Private Enterprise: BLOCKED iap_jsonrpc https://extract.api.odoo.com/...` in `/opt/odoo/instances/obliq/logs/odoo.log` at the moment of failure. Same warning had been silently absorbing Odoofin bank-dashboard + Partner Autocomplete dnb calls throughout April + May.
- Fix shipped end-to-end on Obliq: `pg_dump -Fc` insurance backup (21 MB) → addon directory permanently removed → `iap_account.invoice_ocr.account_token` set NULL (token was bound to pre-Enterprise-activation `database.uuid`) → `systemctl restart odoo-obliq.service` (active in 11s, 206 modules clean, 0 `private_enterprise` mentions in boot log) → HTTPS 200 verified.
- Same procedure ran end-to-end on Oenoteca per user request: 12 MB backup, addon dir removed, 2 stale IAP tokens NULL'd (`partner_autocomplete` from 2026-01-04 + `invoice_ocr` from 2026-01-09), `odoo-oenoteca.service` restarted clean, HTTPS 200 in 1.2 s.
- Latent on the same multi-tenant Hetzner host `ecosire-main-01.ecosire.com` (23.88.13.113): `app` instance still has dormant `private_enterprise` patch in workers (silent until first IAP click); `alvi` keeps it intentionally per Ziad (active Enterprise workaround for alvi-dental).

### 2026-05-09 (late afternoon) — D:/ECOSIRE.COM — generateStaticParams hypothesis tested (round 7) and rejected (round 8 revert)
- Tested the architecture insight surfaced earlier: maybe the Next.js 16 standalone notFound()→200 bug is specifically triggered by `generateStaticParams + dynamicParams=false` (since sister apps don't use that combo and return native 404). Removed both from `/glossary/[slug]` only — small dataset (~75 slugs), low traffic, low risk for an experiment. Commit `8a94bf0d` deployed in round 7 (~5 min).
- Verified live via `scripts/test-glossary-hypothesis.sh`: phantom glossary URLs (e.g. `/glossary/this-term-does-not-exist`) STILL returned HTTP 200 with soft-404 metadata. Identical to pre-removal behavior. **Hypothesis REJECTED**.
- Reverted in round 8 (commit `e6585a25`) to restore the standard pattern (generateStaticParams + dynamicParams=false) for consistency with the other 25 dynamic routes + build-time prerendering of ~825 glossary pages (75 slugs × 11 locales). Verified post-revert: glossary back to baseline.
- Bug source still unknown. Sister apps' working 404 must come from a different difference between ecosire and odovation/muhammadamir. Top candidates: presence of `[...rest]` catch-all in ecosire vs absence in sister apps, Sentry `withSentryConfig` wrap interaction, or some other next.config.ts difference. Each future test = 1 deploy round.
- Cross-project impact: updated `feedback_nextjs_standalone_notfound_status.md` "What does NOT fix it (verified)" list to include "removing generateStaticParams entirely" — saves the next agent from running the same experiment.
- Session totals (D:/ECOSIRE.COM, 2026-05-09): 9 commits across 8 prod deploys. Production state: same as end of morning session — top-level real 404 ✅, slug-level soft-404 metadata ✅, sister apps branded 404 ✅. No regressions introduced by the experiment (revert restored exact pre-experiment state).

### 2026-05-09 (afternoon) — D:/ECOSIRE.COM — Sister apps follow-up: odovation + muhammadamir got friendly not-found.tsx (round 6, 52s deploy)
- Continued the SEO audit work from earlier in the day. Audited `apps/odovation/` and `apps/muhammadamir/` for the same patterns we hit on ecosire.com.
- **Doubled-suffix bug**: NEITHER sister app has it (no page hardcodes their brand suffix). Cleaner than ecosire by accident.
- **404 status**: Both sister apps ALREADY returned real HTTP 404 for unknown URLs at all 3 layers (Cloudflare/Nginx/localhost). They don't have the `[...rest]` catch-all + `generateStaticParams + dynamicParams=false` pattern that triggers the standalone bug on ecosire — Next.js framework default 404 handler works for them natively.
- **Gap addressed**: Both apps lacked any `not-found.tsx` files entirely. Phantom URLs returned 404 status BUT with the layout's homepage default title (e.g. `/blog/this-doesnt-exist` on muhammadamir.com showed `<title>Muhammad Amir — ERP Architect & Technical Consultant | Odoo, AI & Full-Stack</title>`) and bare framework "404: This page could not be found" body. Added `[locale]/not-found.tsx` + root `not-found.tsx` for both apps with branded UI (suggested links Home/Services/Contact for odovation; Home/Services/Blog/Contact for muhammadamir) + soft-404 metadata (`title: 'Page Not Found'` so layout template appends `| ODOVATION` / `| Muhammad Amir`, robots noindex+nofollow+nocache + googleBot noimageindex).
- Round 6 deploy commit `c7987c29` was the fastest of the day — 52s total because turbo cached most builds (only the 2 brand apps had source changes; ecosire-web/api/docs were cache hits).
- Verified live with `scripts/probe-sister-apps-404-v2.sh`: both sister apps now render `<title>Page Not Found | ODOVATION</title>` and `<title>Page Not Found | Muhammad Amir</title>` with noindex robots meta on ALL phantom URLs at all 3 layers. Real homepages still 200 + index/follow.
- **Architecture insight surfaced this round**: sister apps work natively because they DON'T use `generateStaticParams` on their dynamic [slug] routes. The Next.js 16 standalone bug we worked around with proxy.ts allowlist + soft-404 metadata is **specifically triggered by `generateStaticParams` + `dynamicParams = false` on routes wrapped in standalone build**. Removing `generateStaticParams` from ecosire's 26 [slug] routes would be a simpler architectural fix than the proxy.ts allowlist hack — but it needs a performance baseline (Lighthouse mobile/desktop, Cloudflare cache hit %, p50/p95 TTFB) since blog/category/etc. would shift from pre-rendered to SSR-on-demand. Build time would drop ~3 min (no more 13K+ blog page renders). Filed as separate session.
- Cross-project impact: NO new feedback memories needed — the architecture insight is captured in the existing `feedback_nextjs_standalone_notfound_status.md` (already documents which patterns trigger the bug). Sister-apps fix is workspace-local.
- Final SEO audit state for ECOSIRE: ecosire.com top-level 404 ✅, ecosire.com slug-level soft-404 metadata ✅, ecosire.com 14-route doubled-suffix fixed ✅, odovation.com 404 + branded ✅, muhammadamir.com 404 + branded ✅. Total 6 prod deploys today (5 morning code + 1 docs + 1 afternoon code = `032292c3 → 559fec05 → 85224349 → 39218e4b → 7e1592b5 → db0117d7 → c7987c29 → 67870843`).
- Pending NEXT SESSION: real PSI scores once `PAGESPEED_API_KEY` is set; 30-day Search Console deindex monitoring; `/blog` list pagination (half-day); evaluate `generateStaticParams` removal as cleaner alternative to proxy.ts allowlist (separate perf-baseline session).

### 2026-05-09 — D:/ECOSIRE.COM — SEO audit completion: 5 prod deploys, top-level 404 + slug-level soft-404 mitigation + doubled-suffix bug uncovered/fixed
- Continuation of 2026-05-08 SEO audit (47/100, deferred Next.js 16 standalone 404 status bug). 5 prod deploys via self-contained `scripts/deploy-2026-05-09-seo.sh` (uploaded via scp + run remotely, all clean — bypasses the documented Windows PowerShell SSH abort at Step 5).
- **Approach #1 (notFound() in generateMetadata)**: codemod converted 25 of 26 dynamic [slug] routes + catch-all to call notFound() from generateMetadata instead of page body. Theory was that generateMetadata short-circuits earlier in the lifecycle. **Verified ineffective** at all 3 layers (Cloudflare/Nginx/localhost:3000) — Next.js 16 standalone runtime ignores notFound() from generateMetadata too. Commit `032292c3`. Bundled with Phase C: removed 6 duplicate security headers from `apps/web/next.config.ts` (Nginx is canonical at `infrastructure/nginx/ecosire-production.conf:306-312`).
- **Approach #2 (proxy.ts middleware allowlist)**: built explicit `Set<string>` of 39 valid top-level segments + 2 WP legacy 410-Gone routes. For paths whose first post-locale segment isn't allowed, return real `NextResponse(html, {status: 404, headers: {'x-robots-tag': 'noindex'}})`. Self-contained styled minimal HTML body so users don't see ugly text. **Verified working** for top-level URLs at all 3 layers. Commit `559fec05`.
- **Soft-404 metadata (slug-level mitigation)**: not-found.tsx now exports `metadata` with `title: 'Page Not Found'` (layout.template adds `| ECOSIRE`), `robots.index: false`, `robots.follow: false`, `nocache: true`, `googleBot.noimageindex: true`. For slug-level unknowns where status stays 200 due to the Next.js bug, Google reads the meta robots noindex + unique title and treats as 404 for crawl/indexing. Committed in `559fec05` + cosmetic title fix `85224349`.
- **Approach #3 (Nginx body-match rewrite)**: investigated and DEFERRED. Production Nginx 1.24.0 has `--with-http_sub_module` but NO Lua module. sub_filter can rewrite body content but cannot change response status. Lua install (`libnginx-mod-http-lua`) is an infra change; planned maintenance window if soft-404 metadata proves insufficient over 60-day Search Console monitoring.
- **Bonus discovery — doubled `| ECOSIRE | ECOSIRE` title bug** (uncovered during Phase B verification): `[locale]/layout.tsx` exports `title.template: '%s | ECOSIRE'` and 14 dynamic routes hardcoded `| ECOSIRE` in their generateMetadata title, so the layout template appended it again. Examples observed live: `/products/category/marketplace-na` rendered as `North America Marketplaces | Odoo Connectors | ECOSIRE | ECOSIRE`; `/glossary/odoo-connector` rendered as `What Is Odoo Connector? — Definition & Guide | ECOSIRE | ECOSIRE`. Codemod `scripts/strip-doubled-ecosire-suffix.mjs` fixed 13 files / 15 occurrences (`39218e4b`). Industries case had nested template literals + glossary case had `const title = data.seoTitle ?? \`...\`` fallback — both fixed manually (commits `39218e4b` + `7e1592b5`).
- Phase B verification: `scripts/final-real-pages-check.sh` 22-URL spot-check across all 14 dynamic [slug] route types + 5 locale homepages + 4 hub pages — all PASS. Final state: top-level 404 ✅, slug-level soft-404 metadata ✅, real pages single `| ECOSIRE` ✅.
- Cross-project impact: 1 NEW fleet-wide feedback memory captured at workspace-level — `feedback_title_template_double_suffix.md` (when next-intl `[locale]/layout.tsx` exports `title.template '%s | BRAND'`, NEVER append the brand suffix in page-level generateMetadata or it doubles in HTML; grep + codemod patterns included). Generalises to **any** Next.js + next-intl + title.template setup, including the sister apps in the same monorepo (`apps/odovation/`, `apps/muhammadamir/`) which use the same pattern with their own brand suffixes — they should be audited next session. Plus the existing `feedback_nextjs_standalone_notfound_status.md` updated with verified results (approach #1 dead, approach #2 live, soft-404 metadata is the slug-level fix, approach #3 deferred). Sister Next.js 16 standalone workspaces (ECOSIRE.AI frontend, Ad Network Website if upgraded) would benefit from the same proxy.ts allowlist + soft-404 metadata pattern.
- Canonical facts promoted to Unity: none requiring direct vault note edits — all cross-cutting lessons captured as workspace feedback memories. The deploy sequence is reproducible from `~/.claude/projects/D--ECOSIRE-COM/memory/project_seo_audit_2026_05_09.md`.
- Pending NEXT SESSION: real PSI mobile + desktop scores (need PAGESPEED_API_KEY env var on prod for scripted runs); 30-day Search Console monitoring of soft-404 deindex signals; Phase C `/blog` list pagination (half-day, separate session); audit `apps/odovation/` and `apps/muhammadamir/` for the same doubled-suffix pattern. Symptom: `account.move.reversal` in Odoo 19 dropped `refund_method` + `date_mode` fields — `refund_moves()` always creates a DRAFT credit note, no auto-post + auto-reconcile. The v17/v18 idiom of `refund_method='cancel'` for full posted reverse silently fails on v19. Detection signal across the fleet: `account.move` rows with `state='draft' AND reversed_entry_id IS NOT NULL` = stuck reversals from incomplete v17/v18→v19 backports. Affects Quicken Wayfair payout reversals, Suleman Remittance reversal chains, Obliq RMA flows, and any of the 200+ store-management modules with customer-return paths. Sister to existing `feedback_odoo19_xmlrpc_field_renames.md` — both are part of the v19 schema-tightening pass.

  - `feedback_pick_journal_treasury_config_first.md` — when multiple journals share a currency, JE engine and dashboard must use the same source of truth via the operator-facing wrapper table (e.g. `remittance.account`).  Generalises to ANY Odoo module with treasury wrappers (cash management, multi-currency, Bitcoin module, payroll-treasury).  Symptom of divergence: "X currency missing from dashboard" when the JE engine actually posted to a different journal in same currency.
  - `feedback_je_silent_failure_guards_at_jebuilder_boundary.md` — when operators have multiple primitives (kind=cash / bank / conversion + sub-modes) that LOOK applicable but produce different JE shapes, add UserError guards at JE-builder boundaries — NOT more fields, NOT smart auto-routing, NOT more workflow states.  Each error message must list ≥ 2 remediation paths.  Generalises to payroll (gross-net flip), inventory (move types), purchase 3-way matching variants, sale (deposit / progress invoice / advance payment), manufacturing (split / merge / unbuild), accounting (variance / writeoff / writeback).
  - `feedback_monetary_widget_chip_styling_only_last_span.md` — Odoo Monetary widget readonly mode renders BOTH digits AND currency code as direct child spans.  A SCSS rule using `> span:not(.o_field_translate)` blanket-matches BOTH and applies chip styling to the digits.  Always qualify with `:last-child:not(:only-child)` so only the currency suffix gets subdued treatment.  Multi-character codes (AED / USDT / GBP / NGN) are the affected case.

### 2026-05-08 (afternoon) — D:/Development — Quicken Wayfair v19.0.3.14.0: fee + adjustment JEs split by invoice_date (matching principle)
- Quicken team flagged that fee + adjustment JEs were posting on `payout_date` instead of `invoice_date` — wrong fiscal period. Their bookkeeper had been manually editing ~70 JE dates per quarter to compensate (every payout's fee/adj JE was bookkeeper-corrected from May/Apr payout date back to Feb-Mar 2026 invoice date).
- Root cause: CSV parser at `edi_parser.py:235` extracted `invoiceDate` per line but the wizard never passed it through to `wayfair.payout.transaction.processed_at` (NULL on every txn). `_post_settlement_entries` Step 3+4 always used `self.payout_date` for the single aggregate Fee + Adjustment JEs.
- v19.0.3.14.0 patch (deployed prod + backported v18+v17 + 4 GitHub branches pushed): (1) new `_parse_wayfair_date` static method on wizard with defensive DD/MM/YYYY → MM/DD/YYYY → ISO YYYY-MM-DD parse chain — verified Wayfair uses **DD/MM/YYYY** (`05/03/2026` in their CSV is March 5, matching the ~60-day Wayfair settlement cycle, not May 3); (2) wizard + API import now set `processed_at` from parsed CSV `invoiceDate`; (3) `_post_settlement_entries` Step 3 (fees) + Step 4 (adjustments) now group txns by `processed_at::date` and post one aggregate JE per unique date; (4) new `_get_je_date_for_txn` helper falls back to `payout_date` when `processed_at` NULL (legacy txns); (5) `_post_aggregate_je` accepts optional `date` parameter (default `payout_date` for backward compat with suspense-entry call sites). Per-line Clearing Payments + Bank Transfer remain on `payout_date` (cash-flow events). GitHub `ecosire/wayfair_store_management` `main` + `19.0` at `41d1bac`, `18.0` at `cccef2a`, `17.0` at `6a290e6`. Module backup `/opt/odoo-one/_module_backups/wayfair_store_management.bak_pre_v3_14_20260508_105139/`. Pre-flight pg_dump `/tmp/soovah1_pre_v3_14_20260508_104930.dump` (55 MB).
- Major rabbit hole averted: initial proxy attempt for retroactive backfill on the 5 May payouts (id 36-40) used `sale_order.date_order` (customer order date / Wayfair PO date, ~60 days before payout — gave Feb-Mar dates that LOOKED right but were the wrong reason); then second proxy `payout_date - 1 day` (May 3, MM/DD interpretation — also wrong, would have created off-by-2-months errors). Realized the bookkeeper had ALREADY correctly applied DD/MM-interpreted invoice_date for 3 months of payouts. Undid all 20 retroactive moves on payouts 36-40 (10 reversals + 10 new entries on May 3), left bookkeeper's correct entries intact. NO retroactive fix on existing 35 posted payouts — bookkeeper's manual corrections already in place; v3.14.0 only kicks in for NEW imports going forward.
- Cross-project impact: 1 NEW fleet-wide feedback memory captured in D:/Development that applies to ANY platform-store settlement reconciler:
  - `feedback_marketplace_fee_period_matching_principle.md` — for any wayfair / amazon / shopify / ebay / walmart / target+ / ozon / kaufland reconciler, marketplace fees + adjustments must post in the period of the underlying invoice (matching principle), NOT the payout_date. Verify CSV date format per platform — Wayfair uses DD/MM/YYYY despite being US-based. Use `_get_je_date_for_txn` helper pattern with payout_date fallback. Don't proxy from `sale_order.date_order` (customer order date, off by ~60 days) or `payout_date - 1 day` (only matches some platforms). The CSV is the only authoritative source — capture at parse time. Generalises across the 200+ Ecosire store-management module fleet.
- Canonical facts promoted to Unity: [[Quicken Accounting]] / [[Soovah Wayfair]] now at `wayfair_store_management v19.0.3.14.0` with per-invoice-date fee + adjustment posting. Bookkeeper no longer needs manual JE date editing for future imports.
- Pending NEXT SESSION: Quicken team to verify the next payout import (next Wayfair wire) lands fees + adjustments on the correct invoice_date automatically. Demo server (37.27.2.10) Wayfair subdomain still v3.12.x — refresh on next demo cycle.

Setting the code alone is INERT until the cron phones home — service restart does not trigger validation. Heredoc syntax: `odoo shell` must be the first positional arg after the binary, not at the end (`unrecognized parameters: shell` if put at end). Always run as the OS user that owns the filestore (`odoo-obliq`/`odoo`), never `root`/`bitnami`/`daemon`. Does NOT apply to Odoo.sh-hosted DBs (Odoo manages activation server-side). ### 2026-05-08 — D:/Development — Quicken Wayfair payout 10002004819529 rescued + module v19.0.3.13.0 ships robust settlement matcher
- Quicken (https://odoo.soovah.com/, Hetzner `5.78.207.108`, Docker Odoo 19, db `soovah1`): payout 10002004819529 (id=45, date 2026-03-02) was stuck in `imported` state since 2026-05-06. Three root causes intersected: (a) Wayfair CSV header was malformed — extra trailing commas around the reference column made the parser see `PaymentAmount=0.0`; the wizard fell back to summing transaction lines so net_amount=$4,865.20 ended up correct, but `payout_reference_id` got stored as `10002004819529,,,,,,,,,,,,`. (b) `auto_post_settlement = False` on the wayfair instance (was True at 04-06 setup but flipped off at some point) — so the import wizard skipped its `if instance.auto_post_settlement: payout._post_settlement_entries()` branch, stranding the payout. (c) The matcher `_find_invoice_for_txn` Strategy 3 used `('ref', '=', source_order_id)` so invoices with the prefixed `ref='Wayfair-PO-CS630789281'` never matched bare-PO settlement lines, and Strategy 2 missed because the 10 older Jan-2026 SOs (id 61960-62104) lack a populated `wayfair_order_id` field on the sale.order record. An earlier successful posting on 2026-05-05 20:55 (22 moves, balance 0.00) had been MANUALLY REVERSED 40 seconds later via the Reverse Settlement button.
- Repair (3 cleanup passes + module patch): pre-flight `pg_dump` to `/tmp/soovah1_pre_payout_45_fix_20260508_100937.dump` (55 MB). **Pass A**: cleaned reference, re-enabled `auto_post_settlement`, ran `_post_settlement_entries` — state=posted, balance=0.00, 22 moves; 13 of 20 lines went to suspense ($2,894.71 stuck). **Pass B** (`quicken_cleanup_suspense.py`): reconciled 13 suspense txns via `('ref', 'ilike', source_order_id)` matching but used `Move.search(..., limit=1)` so several first-found invoices got over-paid; settled $1,745.42, $1,149.29 still stuck. **Pass C** (`quicken_cleanup_v2.py`): targeted the 9 remaining open-AR invoices by exact name and drained the residual $1,149.30 from suspense to AR. Final state: payout 45 = `posted`, clearing_balance_check=`0.00`, 44 GL moves linked, all 27 customer invoices for these POs `paid` (was 7 paid + 20 not_paid before the rescue), suspense net 0, BNK1 holding $4,865.20 awaiting the bank wire.
- **Module v19.0.3.13.0 patch** (deployed prod + backported v18+v17 + 4 GitHub branches pushed): `_find_invoice_for_txn` rewritten with three improvements — Strategy 2 also matches sale.order via `client_order_ref` = bare PO OR `'Wayfair-PO-<PO>'` (catches older SOs missing `wayfair_order_id`); Strategy 3 changed `('ref', '=', ref)` to `('ref', 'ilike', ref)` and same for `name` (catches `Wayfair-PO-CS630789281` ref when given `CS630789281`); both strategies now wrap results through `_pick(matches)` helper that prefers exact `amount_total == txn.amount` match (via `float_compare` on company currency rounding) for split-shipment cases (one PO → multiple Odoo invoices). Smoke-tested on prod against 5 still-open Wayfair-PO- prefixed invoices: 5/5 matcher returned correct invoice (was 0/5 before). GitHub `ecosire/wayfair_store_management` `main` + `19.0` at `2cf688b`, `18.0` at `6c2346c`, `17.0` at `88d1aae`. Module backup `/opt/odoo-one/_module_backups/wayfair_store_management.bak_pre_v3_13_20260508_102300/`.
- Cross-project impact: 1 NEW fleet-wide feedback memory captured in D:/Development that applies to ANY platform-store settlement reconciler (wayfair / amazon / shopify / ebay / walmart / target+ / ozon / kaufland / etc.):
  - `feedback_settlement_matcher_ilike_and_amount_exact.md` — for any `_find_invoice_for_txn`-style helper, (a) use `ilike` on `invoice.ref` to handle prefixed external identifiers (`Wayfair-PO-`, `Amazon-MFN-`, `Shopify-Order-`, `eBay-Item-` etc.) — `=` exact-match BREAKS the moment integration evolves to prefix the ID in invoice ref; (b) when multiple invoices match one PO (split-shipment cases), prefer one with `amount_total == txn.amount` via `float_compare`, otherwise `limit=1` over-pays the first match while later settlement lines drop to suspense or double-pay. Pattern verified working on Quicken prod 2026-05-08. Generalises across the entire 200+ Ecosire store-management module fleet.
- Canonical facts promoted to Unity: [[Quicken Accounting]] / [[Soovah Wayfair]] now at `wayfair_store_management v19.0.3.13.0`; `auto_post_settlement` re-enabled on instance; payout 10002004819529 fully reconciled. No new server, client, or credentials to add.

### 2026-05-07 (night→05-08 early hours) — D:/Development — Suleman Remittance: v10.1.6 → v10.1.7 → v10.1.8 chain closes form-side gaps in v10.1.0 redesign; both DBs wiped + UI runbook shipped
- Three back-to-back patches deployed clean to BOTH `remtest` AND `remittanceaccounting` (PROD) on Hetzner Bitnami 52.28.45.137. **v10.1.6**: conversion form was binding rate to `exchange_rate` but `_je_conversion` reads `self.fx_rate` — UI-entered rates never reached the JE (TXN/00080 in remtest only worked because the test driver set `fx_rate` directly via `create()`). Rebound view to `fx_rate`, extended `_onchange_prefill_fx_rate` and `_onchange_recompute_converted_amount` to cover `kind='conversion'` so today's Odoo spot rate pre-fills (≈ 1.1765 USD/EUR for Daleel) and "USD Received" auto-recomputes live as `amount × fx_rate`. **v10.1.7**: per Suleman directive *"instead of keeping payee empty if we select company name like Daleel General will it also add to our treasury right?... Make sure we can do both ways"* — added `_is_treasury_partner` helper + `_normalised_parties` wrapper used at top of `_compute_direction`, `_je_cash_kind`, `_je_cash_in`, `_je_cash_out`, `_je_cash_out_on_behalf` so picking the company partner record produces byte-for-byte identical JE shape to leaving the field empty (smoke-tested via odoo shell: `SHAPES EQUAL? True`). Previously the company-partner choice dragged JE engine into the dual-leg branch (DR Daleel-AR / CR Bel Junes-AR — broken accounting against ourselves) and `_compute_direction` flipped `in` → `out` under bridge↔client rules. **v10.1.8**: TXN/2026/00005 (Bel Junes 20k EUR bank deposit, payee=Daleel via the v10.1.7 normalisation) sat in `closed` with `odoo_move_id` empty — Bel Junes balance stuck at +20k EUR. Root cause: `action_advance_stage` only fired `_post_gl_for_kind` when crossing INTO `funds_received`, and `direct_gl=False` (legacy default) made `_post_gl_for_kind` return `False` (defer to invoice flow); when operator subsequently ticked `direct_gl=True` and advanced to `closed`, the JE never got a second chance. Fix: idempotent retry on every forward stage past `funds_received` when `odoo_move_id` empty AND kind is direct-GL eligible (carve-out: `bank+in+direct_gl=False` is the legitimate invoice flow). Plus `direct_gl` default flipped from False to True for the v10.1.0+ redesign reality.
- Both DBs wiped of test transactions via odoo shell (9 deleted on remtest covering TXN/00078–00093 + 3 on `remittanceaccounting` covering TXN/00009–00011); `account.move` + lines deleted, allocations CASCADE, `ir.sequence remittance.transaction` reset to 1, treasury accounts (EUR Bank / EUR Cash / USD Bank / AED Cash) verified at 0 across both DBs. Pre-wipe pg_dumps at `/home/bitnami/dumps/{remtest,remittanceaccounting}_pre_wipe_20260507_163743.dump` plus per-version pre-deploy dumps and module `_module_backups/remittance_management.bak_pre_v10_1_{6,7,8}_*/`.
- Back-fill posted move 367 for TXN/00005 (DR EUR Bank 23,529.41 USD-eq / CR Bel Junes AR 23,529.41 USD-eq, ac=20,000 EUR) — Bel Junes balance verified at `0.00 EUR / 0.01 USD-eq` (forex rounding artefact, harmless).
- UI runbook shipped at `D:/EcosireClients/ActiveClients/Suleman-Remittance/docs/06-runbooks/2026-05-07-case1-case2-ui-guide.md` — Case 1 (3 hops) + Case 2 (6 hops) field-by-field walkthrough with expected JE tables and balance checks per hop, including v10.1.6 + v10.1.7 equivalence notes. Suleman to walk it on remtest next session, then replicate on PROD.
- Cross-project impact: 3 NEW fleet-wide feedback memories captured in D:/Development that apply to ANY Odoo workspace doing model redesign + form rebinding work:
  - `feedback_form_je_field_alignment.md` — when a model is rewritten with new kind catalog or lifecycle, audit ALL fields the form binds vs what each JE method reads. Mismatch produces silent post-failures invisible from UI but visible as `odoo_move_id` empty + partner balances stuck. Test scripts that `create({...})` with all fields pre-filled hide form-binding bugs — smoke-test via UI not just scripts. Generalises to any Odoo module mid-redesign.
  - `feedback_company_partner_normalization.md` — treasury-side fields with "empty = us" semantics must accept BOTH empty AND `company_id.partner_id` as the same input. Pattern: `_is_treasury_partner(p)` helper + `_normalised_parties()` wrapper used at top of every branching method (compute, JE, dispatchers). Field values stay untouched (operator's explicit choice preserved for display); only local branching variables see normalised values. Generalises beyond remittance: expense reports (vendor field empty vs picking own company), inter-company transfers, purchase/sale orders booked against own-company contacts.
  - `feedback_je_post_fallback_retry.md` — JE-post triggers bound to a SINGLE stage transition AND an operator-toggleable boolean = silent skip on toggle-after. Sequence: operator advances tx with boolean=False → JE handler returns False (deferred) → operator ticks boolean True → operator advances past post-target → terminal-stage gate lets it through (boolean is now True) → no retry → tx in terminal with no JE. Fix: idempotent retry (`if odoo_move_id: return self.odoo_move_id` guard at top + `elif` block in `action_advance_stage` covering every forward stage past the post-target). Generalises to any state-machined Odoo workflow gating JE post on a boolean — purchase order confirmation, sale delivery, manufacturing order completion.
- Canonical facts promoted to Unity: none requiring direct vault note edits (Suleman client status, server, credentials reference unchanged; module version delta is workspace-local and captured in D:/Development memory + Suleman-Remittance client folder README). The 3 feedback patterns above are cross-cutting and agents in any workspace working on Odoo redesigns / treasury workflows / state-machined GL posting should consult them.

  - `feedback_purchase_uom_force_via_create_write.md` — onchange override is fragile (form path only); harden with `@api.model_create_multi create()` + `write()` for full coverage (RFQ import, scripted, copy, XML-RPC).
  - `feedback_constrains_relax_to_draft_state.md` — any `@api.constrains` on a transactional model should usually scope to pre-confirm states; chatter writes on confirmed records still fire constraint and break UX.
  - `feedback_iap_extract_keyerror_status_means_no_credits.md` — `result['status']` KeyError in iap_extract = no IAP credits/subscription, NOT a code bug; connect IAP, don't patch the code.
- Canonical facts promoted to Unity: none requiring direct vault note edits (Obliq client status, server, credentials reference are unchanged; module version delta is workspace-local and captured in D:/Development memory + Obliq client folder README). The 4 feedback patterns above are cross-cutting and agents in any workspace working on Odoo product/PO/constraint/IAP issues should consult them.

- Drops the v10.0.11 partner-type-aware sign flip. Suleman's directive: *"negative sign with red color was preferred"*. The earlier "clients flipped, bridges raw GL" model was accounting-correct but read backwards in operator UX — a bridge holding 10k EUR of operator cash showed +10,000 when his mental model was "negative + red = open obligation". TXN/2026/00085 (Muhammad → Suleman Estonia 1k EUR cash internal) now correctly shows Suleman Estonia at -1,000 EUR red. Partner-pair pre-fills explicitly NOT extended (those caused the original self-loop). Three pre-fills shipped: EUR currency default for cash + bank kinds, simplified_data_entry_mode auto-on for cash + bank, commission_pct chain (per-user → company-wide fallback). ### 2026-05-07 (early hours) — D:/Development — Suleman Remittance v10.1.3 ships simultaneous AR + Treasury conversion; Treasury after Case 2 now settles to operator profit only (0 EUR / 0 USD / 915.20 AED)
- Follow-on after v10.1.2 end-session: user flagged v10.1.2's Case 2 ended with Treasury stuck at +10k EUR / -11k USD / +915 AED. Books were technically correct (claims cleared, equity = profit) but cash was split across currencies because the v10.1.0 on-behalf-of conversion was AR-only — the partner's claim flipped EUR→USD but bank cash never moved. User's directive: "when payments are cleared we should not have anything in treasury."
- v10.1.3 extends `_je_conversion` so when `on_behalf_of_partner_id` is set, it posts a 4-line JE at the operator-quoted rate: DR Source AR + CR Target AR + CR Source Bank + DR Target Bank. Both pairs balance in their own currencies; no FX margin plug on the conversion JE itself (operator earnings come from explicit commission lines on later cash-out hops, not from quote-vs-spot spreads on the conversion). Falls back to AR-only with a logged warning when bank journals don't exist for either currency.
- After hop 2.3 in fresh Case 2 run: Bank EUR 10k → 0, Bank USD 0 → +11k, Sul Ko AR EUR cleared, Sul Ko AR USD = 11k. Hop 2.4 then drains Bank USD to 0 — no overdraft. After all 6 hops: Treasury = 0 / 0 / 915.20 AED (= 805.20 commission + 110 AED cross-ccy plug = pure operator profit). All AR = 0.
- Also: list-view totals removed from `views/remittance_transaction_views.xml` (cross-currency sums of EUR + USD + AED into a fake USD total were misleading per Suleman feedback). Per-currency totals remain on Balances + Treasury dashboards.
- Both DBs wiped (`remtest` + `remittanceaccounting`) and re-tested cleanly with the new conversion pattern. HTTP 200 verified on both. Pre-deploy backup `_module_backups/remittance_management.bak_pre_v10_1_3_*`.
- Cross-project impact: NEW fleet-wide feedback memory `feedback_on_behalf_of_conversion_simultaneous_ar_treasury_flip.md` — canonical pattern for any future payment-facilitation module (remittance / hawala / FX bureau / multi-currency wallet). Documents the wrong AR-only model, the right simultaneous-flip model, and the operational symptoms when this is misimplemented (treasury currency drift, phantom overdrafts after chains clear).

> Every Claude Code session — in any workspace — writes a 1–5 line entry here on close via the `hive-mind-sync` skill. Entries are reverse-chronological. This file is the single thread that connects all project workspaces into one continuous conversation for future agents.

## How to write an entry

Keep entries tight. Format:

```
### YYYY-MM-DD — Workspace name — one-line headline
- What was done (1–3 lines, outcomes not process)
- Cross-project impact, if any (mentions of other workspaces)
- Canonical facts promoted to Unity: [[wiki-links to updated notes]]
```

## What belongs here (vs. project-local memory)

**Write here** when the work touches more than one workspace, produces a canonical fact (client/server/credential), or would be useful to an agent in a DIFFERENT project next week.

**Keep in project-local memory** when the work is only about that codebase's internals — a fix to a specific file, a local test failure, a refactor inside one module. Those stay in `~/.claude/projects/<slug>/memory/`.

---

## Log (newest first)

### 2026-05-08 (night) — D:/Development — Suleman Remittance v10.1.17: cross-currency field promotion to cash/bank
- Suleman flagged TXN/2026/00006 (cross-ccy cash IN: 80k AED clearing 22k USD AR) and TXN/2026/00007 (cross-ccy cash OUT: 39k AED clearing remaining 11k USD AR) had no record of the USD amount being converted: *"on scale with multiple client transactions it will cause issue."* Audit blind spot: target_currency_id + converted_amount + exchange_rate were treated as kind=conversion-only on the form view, even though the underlying fields are general-purpose. JE engine for cross-ccy cash IN/OUT computed the cleared other-ccy amount but never wrote it back to the tx record.
- Shipped v10.1.17 (5 changes in one release): JE-engine writeback in 3 builders (`_writeback_cross_ccy_fields` helper); form view "Currency Conversion" → "Currency Detail" with `invisible="not target_currency_id"` so same group renders for both kinds; operator pre-fill validation guard via `_check_operator_preset_target_ccy` (third silent-miss guard layered on v10.1.11 + v10.1.16); `funds_origin_hint` Char compute walks `source_transaction_id` chain (max 5 hops) for cash/bank OUT; backfill script populated 2 historic rows on remtest (TXN/00006 + TXN/00007 → USD/11000.00 each).
- Both DBs LIVE at 19.0.10.1.17 / installed (HTTPS 303 in 2.3s). Pre-flight pg_dumps preserved.
- GitHub: `engrmuhammadamirnazir/remittance_management` `main` + `19.0` + tag `v19.0.10.1.17` all at `629357f`. Pushed BEFORE deploy as belt-and-suspenders.
- Cross-project impact: NEW fleet feedback `feedback_promote_existing_fields_over_parallel_ones.md` — when a model field family already exists for one kind/case and a similar display need arises, prefer relaxing visibility + writeback over creating parallel fields. Single semantic vocabulary, list-view filterability free, smaller diff. Applies anywhere features grew kind-by-kind: sale order kind-only fields, stock move outgoing-only fields, account move invoice-only fields, marketplace platform-specific fields with overlapping protocols.
- Canonical facts promoted to Unity: [[Remittance — Salueman Arif]] bumped to v19.0.10.1.17.

### 2026-05-05 evening — D:/Development + D:/EcosireClients — Future Vision ZATCA Phase 2 + Phase 3 LIVE on production for ABIR ALMANAFETH
- **The blocker from 2026-05-05a (Simplified XAdES signing bug) RESOLVED.** Three precision corrections in `build_xmldsig_signature()` of `zatca_phase2.py` (+81/−34 in single function): (A) `<xades:CertDigest>/<ds:DigestValue>` = SHA-256 over the BASE64 ASCII text bytes of the cert, NOT raw DER bytes; (B) SP-ref digest = SHA-256 over an Alhaditech-format raw string with `xmlns:xades` on SP itself + redundant `xmlns:ds` on every ds: child + SDK indentation (32→36→40→44→48→52 spaces) + LF line endings, NOT lxml C14N output; (C) `<ds:X509IssuerName>` = `", ".join(rdn.rfc4514_string() for rdn in reversed(cert.issuer.rdns))`. Standard scenarios passed before fix because `/clearance/single` overwrites client signature server-side; Simplified `/reporting/single` validates byte-for-byte. Recipe locked via SDK 238-R4.0.0 Simplified Credit Note reference + Alhaditech `ksa_zatca_integration` paid Odoo connector reference; verified byte-equal via 4 layered scripts in `tmp/diff/`. 21/21 unit tests pass.

### 2026-05-03 (Suleman Remittance v10.0.39 → v10.0.40 — IAS 21 FX gain/loss fix on cross-currency invoice payment) — D:/Development — solves the deferred partial-paid + EUR Bank -2,700 bug
- **Trigger:** user asked me to act as expert accountant and solve the deferred FX-residual bug from v10.0.27.
- **Root cause:** v10.0.27 `_create_odoo_payment` (step-6 hawala JE) wrote `debit = self.total` (foreign EUR numerical value) while setting `currency_id = EUR` but NOT populating `amount_currency`. Odoo's invariant is that `debit`/`credit` are ALWAYS in COMPANY currency; the foreign-currency leg lives in `amount_currency` (signed). Without `amount_currency`, the foreign leg defaults to 0. On Daleel (USD-functional) processing 15k EUR: step-4 invoice's AR was @ 17,647.06 USD / +15,000 EUR; step-6 cleared AR @ 15,000 USD / 0 EUR (treating foreign as company). `reconcile()` saw foreign mismatched and couldn't trigger Odoo's exchange-move generation, leaving 2,647.06 USD residual → `payment_state='partial'`. Same gap manifested as -2,700 EUR phantom on Bank dashboard.
- **Fix:** rewrote builder using `foreign_ccy._convert(amount, company_ccy, company, date_ref)` for proper company-currency conversion + `amount_currency` populated (signed) on every line. `reconcile()` now auto-creates the FX exchange move per **IAS 21 §28** (exchange differences arising on settlement at rates different from initial recognition shall be recognised in P&L) — posts to `company.income_currency_exchange_account_id` (gain, acct id 27) or `expense_currency_exchange_account_id` (loss, acct id 38). Both pre-configured on Daleel during initial COA install.
- GitHub `engrmuhammadamirnazir/remittance_management` `main 184fd59 → 9d099f6` + tag v19.0.10.0.40 (NO AI attribution per client-repo rule). Both DBs at `installed | 19.0.10.0.40` HTTPS 303.
- Pending: existing partial-paid invoices on remittanceaccounting (if any) need manual un-reconcile + re-reconcile from Accounting → Reporting → Partner Ledger (NOT auto-migrated; pairing requires accountant judgement).
- Cross-project impact: ONE new fleet-wide rule [[feedback_amount_currency_required_on_multi_ccy_je]] — sister to [[feedback_je_foreign_amount_as_company_debit_credit]] + [[feedback_aggregator_currency_axis_bug]] + [[feedback_kind_blind_compute_on_stored_field]]. Same family: explicit currency-axis handling required at multi-currency boundaries. Applies to every Odoo module that constructs multi-currency journal entries programmatically (bank statement importers, custom payment wizards, inter-company transfers, FX/MTO/hawala settlement flows, foreign-currency landed costs).
- Canonical fact promoted to Unity: `04 - Resources/Patterns/feedback_amount_currency_required_on_multi_ccy_je.md`.

- **Trigger:** user hit `Invalid Operation. Upload TT copy first` mid-demo-video; cascaded into 6 more bugs in same recording window. All shipped end-to-end on both DBs in one continuation, GitHub `main 184fd59` + tag v19.0.10.0.39.
- **7 fixes:** (1) `AttributeError 'fees'` on `_je_outbound_hawala` — `self.fees` was wrong field, corrected to `self.commission_amount` (pre-existing v10.0.30 bug, never triggered until user advanced bank_usd_out); (2) NEW `remittance.upload.tt.wizard` — file picker + Confirm in one popup, button "5. Confirm TT Upload" → "5. Upload TT Copy" opens wizard, bypasses for invoices already with attachment; (3) Bridge fix — `remittance.invoice.create()` now stamps `remittance_invoice_id` reverse-link on tx immediately (TXN/2026/00026 symptom of "no invoice generated" on completed-flow tx), migration backfills existing rows; (4) "Hawala spread" → "Cross-Currency FX & Operator Margin" + 5 tooltip strings rewritten ("Hawaladar-negotiated rate" → "Operator-negotiated rate", etc.); (5) `open_amount` kind-aware — was applying inbound-side `amount - settled` formula to ALL kinds, so closed outbounds had stored open_amount = full amount, inflating list "Open" total to $13,126.18 phantom exposure on 4 closed tx; outbounds now get open_amount=0; (6) `settlement_unsettled` kind-aware (symmetric mirror) — inbounds had full amount as "Unsettled"; same fix block; migration backfills both; (7) PDF reports get proper page-level header/footer — `external_layout_remittance` was hard-coding `<div class="header">`/`<div class="footer">` INSIDE body content (wkhtmltopdf doesn't promote those to page-level), 17 reports affected; rewrote to delegate to `web.external_layout`, all reports now use Daleel's configured Document Layout (primary_color #5e4766 purple, id=206).
- **Codebase audit subagent ran** scanning every compute on remittance.transaction / res.partner / remittance.account / remittance.invoice for the kind-blind compute family. Result: 0 P0/P1 beyond Fix 5/6, 4 P2 missing-`@api.depends` decorators (non-stored, non-blocking, skipped). `.fees` and `.partner_id` cross-model leakage checks: clean.
- **TWO targeted wipes** during the session for clean demo state: bank_eur_in only (after bridge bug discovery), then all 3 bank-flow kinds (after AttributeError + Open-bug). Cash transactions (cash_eur_in/out + cash_aed_in/out) kept for demo continuity. Invoice sequence reset.
- **Pending (unchanged from prior session):** partial-paid invoice + EUR Bank -2,700 — deferred FX-residual bug from v10.0.27 step-6 hawala posting when company ccy ≠ deposit ccy. Needs accountant call for rate-convention + which account carries the spread. Will recur on multi-currency demos.
- Cross-project impact: TWO new fleet-wide rules captured — [[feedback_kind_blind_compute_on_stored_field]] (sister to [[feedback_aggregator_currency_axis_bug]] + [[feedback_je_foreign_amount_as_company_debit_credit]]: store=True computes that aggregate via FK reverse-collections must filter by kind/state when formula semantics fit only a subset; otherwise list-view aggregations show phantom totals) AND [[feedback_qweb_inline_header_no_page_layout]] (inline `<div class="header">` in body content does NOT become a page-level header in wkhtmltopdf — use `t-call="web.external_layout"` so company Document Layout wires `--header-html`/`--footer-html` properly; demonstrated retrofitting 17 reports with a single template edit). Both apply to every Odoo workspace with multi-kind models or custom QWeb reports.

### 2026-05-03 (Hive-Mind infrastructure overhaul — backup pipeline rebuilt + cross-workspace lessons RAG + deploy guard rail) — D:/Development + ~/.claude — fleet-wide
- **Trigger:** user said "make sure those mistakes are not made again, all deployment via proper version control with complete log/history, advance RAG/memory system, skills/agents/custom-settings backup to dedicated GitHub repo". Discovered ~/.claude push had silently failed for **25 days straight** (since 2026-04-08) because a 104.30 MB `.jsonl` blob exceeded GitHub's 100 MB limit. The "lost skill" risk was active and growing.
- **Phase 1 — push pipeline fix:** `pip install git-filter-repo`, ran `git_filter_repo --path-glob 'projects/**/*.jsonl' --invert-paths --force` to strip historical blobs. `.git` shrank 1.2 GB → 25 MB. Rewrote `.gitignore` to exclude `projects/**/*.jsonl`, `subagents/`, `sessions/`, `cache/`, `*.bak`, `.credentials.json`, plus per-workspace `worktrees/`, `runtime/`, `*.lock`. Force-pushed clean main to `engrmuhammadamirnazir/claude`.
- **Phase 2 — workspace backup:** built `~/.claude/scripts/backup_all_workspaces.py` (cross-platform, deletion-aware sync via `os.walk` topdown with in-place dir pruning so it never descends into `node_modules/` / `worktrees/`). First-time sync mirrored 380+ files in 18 seconds: D:/Development (16 MB), D:/ECOSIRE.COM (**101 skills + 20 agents — biggest at-risk store**), D:/ECOSIRE.AI (32 skills + 29 agents), D:/ECOSIRE.IO (8 agents), D:/OpenClaw (lockfile only). Counted **133 skills + 57 agents off-machine for the first time ever.**
- **Phase 3 — lessons RAG:** built `lessons_rebuild.py` that walks every `~/.claude/projects/<ws>/memory/` dir, parses YAML frontmatter, auto-categorizes by 11 patterns (orm/sql/deploy/security/sync/ui/accounting/fleet/git/ux/other) and 4 workspaces. Output: `~/.claude/lessons/INDEX.md` (645 lessons indexed in ~2 sec, fully grep-able), `by-pattern/<p>.md`, `by-workspace/<w>.md`, `by-recent/recent-30-days.md`. Agents now grep one file instead of 506 individual feedback memories.
- **Phase 4 — fleet broadcast (hive-mind LEARNING, not artifact propagation):** initial draft of `fleet_broadcast.py` had 3 modes — `--promote-to-user` (bulk workspace skill/agent → `~/.claude/`), `--broadcast` (ECOSIRE.COM origin → peer workspaces), `--pull-lessons`. **User correctly pushed back:** "propagation of project specific skills and agents is not right approach — learning is." Removed `--broadcast` and bulk `--promote-to-user`; kept `--pull-lessons` (writes read-only `LESSONS.md` into every workspace `.claude/`) and replaced bulk promotion with `--promote-skill <name>` (explicit per-skill, requires reviewing the SKILL.md and consciously deciding it has no workspace-specific encoded conventions). Captured as fleet-wide rule [[feedback_propagate_learning_not_artifacts]]: lessons cross workspace boundaries (the universal pattern); skills/agents stay scoped (the workspace-specific implementation that incidentally encodes the pattern). Sharing what we learned ≠ copying what we built. Avoids bloat, drift, and false uniformity across workspaces.
- **Phase 5 — deploy guard rail:** built `deploy/checklist.py` (pre/post/full subcommands). Pre-deploy: dev tree clean + EcosireSolutions mirror in sync + GitHub branches aligned (main = 19.0) + `.bak_*` not in addons-path + manifest version bumped + pre-backup taken. Post-deploy: HTTPS 200 + login page loads + module state == "installed" + filestore ownership matches `odoo_user`. Codifies every mistake from v10.0.37/38 deploys (REF-vs-NAME wipe, daemon-vs-odoo upgrade user, .bak in addons-path).
- **Phase 6 — Windows scheduled task:** updated `Claude Code Daily Backup` to call `backup-all-workspaces.ps1` → `backup_all_workspaces.py`. Old broken `backup-daily.sh` retired. Push verification baked in (the bug it hid for 25 days won't recur).
- **Phase 7 — Unity promotion:** created `Unity/04 - Resources/Patterns/` with the 8 canonical fleet-wide gotchas from this session. New `PATTERNS - INDEX.md` MOC.
- **Cross-project impact:** every workspace on this machine now (a) has its `.claude/` mirrored daily off-machine, (b) gets a read-only LESSONS.md broadcast of all workspace knowledge, (c) is governed by the deploy guard rail before any module touches prod. The single dedicated repo `engrmuhammadamirnazir/claude` is now the meta-backup for the entire fleet.

### 2026-05-02 (Suleman Remittance v10.0.36 → v10.0.37 → v10.0.38 — read-side aggregator currency-axis fix + write-side bank_eur_out_usd_in pivots to hybrid balance-shift + bank movement; remtest wiped for fresh demo) — D:/Development — 2 versions back-to-back, multi-agent, both prod DBs live
- **Trigger:** user reported on TXN/2026/00021 (Amir 10,000 EUR → 11,800 USD @ 1.18 conversion) Amir's EUR balance dropped by 11,764.71 instead of 10,000.
- **v10.0.37** (`3e1da61`): A1 fixed silent currency-axis bug in `remittance.balance.line` + `remittance.partner.balance` SQL views — switched from `SUM(debit-credit)` (always company currency) to `SUM(amount_currency)` with COALESCE fallback for legacy `account.payment` posts where `amount_currency=0`. The bug had been hidden for years because v9-era `_je_bank_eur_out_usd_in` set `debit = amount` literally; v10.0.36's correct conversion (debit = amount × spot) exposed it. After deploy, Amir EUR reads +15,000.00 ✓. Also shipped: B1 builder uses operator-quoted rate when one foreign side == company ccy (eliminates FX plug in 2-ccy cases); B2 commission_pct ↔ commission_amount bidirectional sync; C1 NEW `remittance.company.solvency` aggregator (per company × ccy: deposits/payouts/net + bank vs liability + solvency delta — mirrors worksheet 'matchup' sheet); C2 Balance Detail drill-down conversion legs render as one multi-column row (src→tgt at rate with margin %); C3 Flow Timeline widget refresh (vertical timeline, kind-colored dots, you-are-here pill, conversion legs show inline rate + margin %). 3 module-developer agents in parallel built C1/C2/C3 in worktrees while controller did A1+B1+B2; all merged clean.
- **v10.0.38** (`a00eaa8`): user observed Treasury still showing 25k EUR after the conversion + clarified "by euro out dollar in means they move that amount from euro account to usd account so it should also show in treasury — it's not cash, it's bank transaction actually". Worksheet review confirmed: per `NEW_BUSINESS_2024_clean.xlsx` 'accounts' sheet column band, conversions are real bank trades. Pivoted `_je_bank_eur_out_usd_in` to **hybrid 4-line JE**: (1) DR Customer Liability EUR sender + (2) CR Bank EUR (operator's EUR cash leaves) + (3) DR Bank USD (operator's USD cash arrives) + (4) CR Customer Liability USD sender (net of any commission), plus optional CR Commission Income line and FX plug for 3-currency cases. Treasury KPI now drops on EUR side and rises on USD side per conversion. Hard pre-conditions: bank journal in EUR + USD must exist with default_account_id set; commission revenue account if commission > 0.
- **remtest WIPED for fresh Suleman demo** — TWO passes: pass 1 by REF pattern caught 16 moves; user reported Treasury still showing 25k → diagnosis: `ref ILIKE 'INV/2026/%'` missed 17 moves whose `ref` was `'Payment for INV/2026/00001'` or `'Reversal of: INV/2026/...'` (descriptive prefix, not journal code). Pass 2 by NAME pattern (`name LIKE 'PREFIX/2026/%'`) cleaned 23 more moves + 60 AMLs + reconcile FK rows. Final state: 0 transactions, all 14 bank/cash journals zero AML balance, 12 partners + 10 accounts kept, sequences reset. Pre-wipe backup `/tmp/pre_v10_0_37_remtest_wipe_20260502_173614.dump`.
- GitHub `engrmuhammadamirnazir/remittance_management` `main 66e9dbc..3e1da61..a00eaa8` + tags v19.0.10.0.37 + v19.0.10.0.38 (NO AI attribution). Both DBs `installed | 19.0.10.0.38` HTTPS 200. Pre-deploy backups ×4 in `/tmp/`.
- Cross-project impact: TWO new hard rules — [[feedback_aggregator_currency_axis_bug]] (fleet-wide gotcha for any custom Odoo SQL aggregator over `account_move_line` that groups by `currency_id`: SUM(amount_currency) NOT SUM(debit-credit); sister to [[feedback_je_foreign_amount_as_company_debit_credit]] read-side counterpart) AND [[feedback_db_wipe_ref_vs_name_pattern]] (when SQL-wiping account.move, match on `name` not `ref` — refs often carry "Payment for X" / "Reversal of: X" prefixes that don't start with the journal code, so REF-based ILIKE leaves orphans). Both reusable across multi-currency partner ledgers, treasury dashboards, FX/MTO modules, demo-prep DB resets fleet-wide.
- Canonical facts promoted to Unity: [[Remittance — Salueman Arif]] bumped to v19.0.10.0.38.

### 2026-05-02 (Suleman Remittance v10.0.32 → v10.0.33 → v10.0.34 → v10.0.35 → v10.0.36 — UX hardening + FX UX + bank_eur_out_usd_in pivot to balance-shift) — D:/Development — 5 back-to-back versions, both prod DBs live
- **v10.0.32** (`6ef9b8a` + hotfix `8b7d72a`): Ledger IN/OUT inversion on Balance Detail drill-down fixed — `get_breakdown` payload now ships sign-flipped `in_amount`/`out_amount` matching the customer-statement POV already used by running totals; pickup-by-code wizard generic "no deposit selected" replaced by `_resolve_inbound_by_code` helper used by both onchange AND `action_release` fallback with specific diagnostics. Migration hotfix: `rp.display_name` (computed) → `rp.name` (stored).
- **v10.0.33** (`6a24f19`): pickup wizard FIFO double-counting collision fixed — `remittance.transaction.create()` was firing `_auto_link_settlement_on_create` and the wizard was ALSO explicitly creating a settlement; constraint saw `already=2×amount` and raised. New `skip_auto_settle=True` context flag bypasses the FIFO hook. Operator's typed MTCN must always win over date-order auto-link.
- **v10.0.34** (`dfc5b6e`): user feedback on EUR↔USD conversion form — "euro to usd or usd to euro is confusing, maybe a clear label will also help". 3 new computed fields surface direction and live spot inline: `fx_pair_label` ("1 EUR = ? USD"), `fx_spot_hint` (live `res.currency.rate`), `fx_deposit_currency_id`. Discovered + fixed Odoo's currency rate cron stuck at `nextcall=2026-04-17` — manually triggered `update_currency_rates` for all 3 companies (CBUAE for Daleel, ECB for OÜ entities), populated 9 rates (EUR 0.85 / USD 1.0 / AED 3.6725).
- **v10.0.35** (`4f01464`): `_je_bank_eur_out_usd_in` v9-era arithmetic bug fixed — old 5-line builder had two compounded bugs (literal foreign amounts used as company-currency `debit/credit`, plus 5th line had no balancing CR). For TXN/2026/00021 the imbalance was exactly 10,000. Replaced with clean 4-line + commission + FX plug.
- **v10.0.36** (`66e9dbc`): user design clarification — "intended balance is for amir USD account and not company account, conversion shuffles client balance from euro to usd, then in last stage usd we actually pay client or beneficiary". Pivoted `bank_eur_out_usd_in` from Mode B (cash-flow) to Mode A (balance-shift, no cash leg). New 3-line JE: `DR Customer Liability EUR (sender) / CR Customer Liability USD (sender) / ± FX margin`. Hard pre-check: sender must hold ≥ amount EUR liability (otherwise raises with directive to deposit first). Documented partner-setup guidance: `partner_payer_id` = customer; `partner_payee_id` = empty or same; "no payee → operator's bank/treasury" rule applies ONLY to cash-out kinds.
- GitHub `engrmuhammadamirnazir/remittance_management` `main 90635e8..6ef9b8a..8b7d72a..6a24f19..dfc5b6e..4f01464..66e9dbc` + 5 new tags v19.0.10.0.32 through v19.0.10.0.36 (NO AI attribution per client-repo rule). FX margin lands on dedicated `remittance_fx_margin_account_id` (per IAS 21 — operator spread is REVENUE not generic FX g/l). 5 new fields including `fx_rate` (operator-quoted, defaults to Odoo spot if 0) + 4 immutable post-post snapshots (`fx_rate_at_post`/`fx_spot_rate_at_post`/`fx_rate_locked_at`/`fx_rate_source`); `write()` guard refuses post-post snapshot mutation; mail.thread audit log on every cross-currency post documenting sender, beneficiary, amounts, rate, source, spot, spread %, and company-currency P&L.

Findings integrated: tightened thresholds 5%/15% (from 10%/25% draft), preferred dedicated `remittance_fx_margin_account_id` over generic `income_currency_exchange_account_id`, added `fx_rate_source` snapshot enum, added `write()` immutability guard. - **3 cross-project hard rules captured** (apply fleet-wide, NOT just to Suleman):
  - `feedback_odoo_bin_run_as_odoo_user_not_daemon.md` — on Bitnami Odoo deployments, `odoo-bin -u` MUST run as `sudo -u odoo` (NOT `daemon`); workers run as `odoo` and can't read filestore objects created by daemon. Symptom: HTTPS 500 on every CSS/JS asset post-upgrade. Hit on the v10.0.28 prod deploy → fixed by `chown -R odoo:odoo` filestore + future upgrades as `sudo -u odoo`. Applies to ALL Bitnami clients (Suleman now, plus any future Bitnami install).

  - `feedback_account_move_double_reversal_creates_phantom.md` — always check existing `reversed_entry_id` matches before invoking the reversal wizard; double-reversing the same posted move creates two opposite-sign reversal entries that don't cancel. Hit during v10.0.28 data correction (BNK1/2026/00006 phantom +25k for partner Amir). Applies to any Odoo workspace doing iterative correction scripts (Oenoteca, Obliq, Sahara client books).

### 2026-05-02 (demo server — shoppingfeed_demo HTTP 500 fix + 204-subdomain audit) — D:/Development → Hetzner CPX42 37.27.2.10 — all 204 demos verified live
- User: "https://shoppingfeed.demo.ecosire.com/web check why demo is not live" → expanded to "make sure all demos are live". Surface said HTTP 200 but POST login crashed: `ValueError: Wrong @depends on '_compute_feed_quality' (compute method of field shoppingfeed.product.feed_quality_score). Dependency field 'product_brand_id' not found in model product.product`. Root cause: `shoppingfeed_store_management/models/shoppingfeed_feed_quality.py:60` had `'odoo_product_id.product_brand_id'` in `@api.depends` even though the runtime body guards with `if 'product_brand_id' in product._fields:` — Odoo's `Registry._field_triggers` is lazy and `resolve_depends` parses the path on the FIRST write to ANY model in the database. Login specifically because login creates `res.users.log` → `modified()` → trigger-tree build → crash. **Option A fix:** removed that one line, bumped manifest 19.0.2.0.0 → 19.0.2.0.1, file backups stamped `*.bak_20260502_081613`, `systemctl restart odoo-demo` clean.
- **204-demo audit via parallel HTTPS POST-login probe** (`/tmp/audit_demos_https.py`, 12-thread pool, ~90 sec) → **204/204 return post=303 → /odoo** (full auth success). False-positive caveat caught: internal-port probes (`127.0.0.1:8069` with `Host:` header) miss `X-Forwarded-Proto: https` and falsely 400 on website-themed modules like `branding`; public-HTTPS path is ground truth.
- **Cross-project hard rule** captured at `D:/Development/.../memory/feedback_api_depends_optional_field.md` — sister to `feedback_module_pump_static_validation_insufficient` from earlier today. ANY `@api.depends('rel.field_provided_by_optional_module')` will lazy-crash the entire database on first write even with runtime hasattr guards. Three fix paths: (A) drop the optional-field path from depends, (B) hard-add the optional module to manifest depends, (C) dynamic depends via `_setup_complete` override. Static validation (`py_compile` + `ET.parse` + `ast.literal_eval`) does NOT catch this — only `odoo-bin -i <module> --stop-after-init` + a triggering write does. Reusable in any Odoo workspace where modules cross-reference fields from other modules.
- **Pending — not yet acted on:** (1) local `D:/Development/odoo19/server/addons/shoppingfeed_store_management/models/` is empty (only `__pycache__`) — same `git filter-branch --msg-filter` damage that hit Remittance this morning per session_2026_05_02e. Demo server is the only intact copy. Needs `scp`-back recovery + EcosireSolutions mirror create + GitHub repo sync of v19.0.2.0.1 fix to all 4 branches. (2) `/var/log/odoo/odoo-demo.log` is 2.4 GB (logrotate not trimming). (3) Fleet-wide grep for `@api.depends('rel.optional_field')` pattern across 215 modules.
- Cross-project impact: the new `feedback_api_depends_optional_field` rule applies to module-developer pumps in any workspace and to any future client module that conditionally enriches behavior when an optional Odoo app is installed.

### 2026-05-02 (Suleman Remittance v10.0.26 + v10.0.27 — bridge between remittance.transaction ↔ remittance.invoice + hawala posting convention) — D:/Development — sender's partner balance now reflects deposit instead of netting to zero
- **User reported "TXN/2026/00008 i did this bank euro in transaction and its not reflecting in muhammad amir balance and also no invoice was created and linked"** — diagnosis: the `bank_eur_in` kind was designed to delegate posting to a parallel `remittance.invoice` record (7-step compliance flow: doc check → compliance → invoiced → TT upload → bank notified → paid → handed over), but the two models had NO link between them, no UX surfaced the second half from the transaction form, and nothing prevented closing a transaction without its invoice. Zero `remittance.invoice` records existed on remtest — the parallel system had never been used. TXN/2026/00008 walked from draft to closed with `odoo_move_id=NULL` → no JE → no balance change → no invoice document.
- **v10.0.26 — Bridge** between the two models. 3 new fields: `remittance.transaction.remittance_invoice_id` m2o, `remittance.invoice.transaction_id` m2o (domain-filtered to bank_eur_in + invoice mode), `remittance.transaction.direct_gl` Boolean toggle (skip the invoice flow entirely and post a cash-style JE for casual bank receipts). UI: 2 header buttons ("✚ Create Invoice" / "📄 Open Linked Invoice") with pre-fill context, "Invoice Workflow" group on the form, stage-advance guard (closing bank_eur_in invoice-mode requires linked invoice in {paid, handed_over}), bidirectional auto-stamp (when invoice posts step-4 GL move, transaction's `odoo_move_id` auto-populates + AML rows tagged with `remittance_tx_id`). Bridge mechanically working but Amir's balance still 0 because standard `out_invoice → payment` flow nets receivable to zero.
- **User clarified mid-session: "hawala Business this invoice is for record purposes and balance management is for remittance management purposes, so make sure your design intelligently does both parts."** This was the design-defining moment — separated concerns: customer invoice = audit/client document, partner balance = operational remittance truth.
- **v10.0.27 — Hawala posting convention.** Rewrote `remittance.invoice._create_odoo_payment` (step 6 — Money Arrived) as ONE atomic 4-line journal entry: `DR Bank (total) / CR Customer AR (total — clears step-4 invoice) / DR Service Income (principal only — NO partner_id) / CR Customer Deposit Liability (principal only — partner=sender)`. Net effect after the full 7-step flow: Bank +total, AR cleared, Service Income +fees only (proper hawala revenue recognition where principal is passthrough not income), Customer Liability +principal partner-tagged to the sender (operational balance reflects funds held for onward remittance). Reuses existing `res.company.remittance_client_payable_account_id` (account 489 / code 210100, `liability_payable` — already configured on Suleman's chart from v9 setup). Service Income account resolved by reading from POSTED out_invoice's `invoice_line_ids` (Odoo's `_compute_account_id` resolves from chart defaults at posting time → product property is empty even when posting works correctly).
- **Critical implementation detail captured as new gotcha:** Income reclassification line MUST NOT carry `partner_id`. Attempt 1 had it on all 4 lines → `remittance.balance.line` aggregator (which sums `debit - credit` GROUPED BY `partner_id × currency_id`, regardless of account_id) saw a wash for the sender → balance still 0. Attempt 2 removed partner_id from the Income line only, kept it on Bank/AR/Liability → balance flipped to +25,000. Pattern: when building multi-line JEs that span account types, only PARTNER ACTIVITY lines (AR, AP, Customer Liability per sender) get partner_id; COMPANY ACTIVITY lines (Bank, Income, Expense, Suspense, FX margin) leave it empty.
- **TXN/2026/00008 walked end-to-end** under v10.0.27 (after reversing the v10.0.26 buggy moves via `account.move.reversal` wizard, which preserves audit trail vs direct unlink). Final state: Amir's EUR partner balance reads **+25,000.00** in the Balances dashboard. Move trail in `BNK1/2026/00004`: 4 lines as designed.
- **GitHub `engrmuhammadamirnazir/remittance_management` `d4186fe..1ba66b4..13b887d` + tags v19.0.10.0.26 + v19.0.10.0.27** (NO AI attribution per client-repo rule). Both prod DBs (`remtest` + `remittanceaccounting`) at `installed | 19.0.10.0.27` HTTP 200. All 4 working trees aligned: dev tree, EcosireSolutions mirror, GitHub canonical clone, prod. Pre-deploy backups ×4: `/tmp/pre_v10_0_2{6,7}_{remtest,remittanceaccounting}_2026050{2_082542,2_085359,2_091142}.dump`.
- **Cross-project gotcha #1 — Income reclassification lines must NOT carry partner_id.** Any custom JE that mixes account types where the same partner appears on offsetting sides — partner-tag ONLY the operational-balance line. The other side is a company-level wash. Reusable in any Odoo workspace with custom partner-balance views (remittance, payment processors, escrow, prepaid services).
- **Cross-project gotcha #2 — Resolve income/AR account from POSTED invoice lines, not product properties.** `product.property_account_income_id` is the override — Odoo's chart default frequently fills in at posting time, so the property stays empty even when the invoice posted correctly. For custom JEs that mirror a posted account, read it from `account.move.invoice_line_ids` AFTER `action_post()`.
- **Cross-project reference — `account.move.reversal` wizard pattern** for un-posting committed moves while preserving audit trail. Useful for code-change-driven re-postings, demo data cleanup, wrong-account corrections without `unlink`. The wizard auto-handles unreconcile + re-reconcile of the reversal pair.
- **Pending v10.0.28 — Outbound side asymmetry.** When a sender's deposit is paid out via `cash_eur_out` / `bank_usd_out`, the existing `_je_cash_out` posts `DR Payee AR / CR Cash` — leaving the sender's Liability uncleared. Books temporarily asymmetric (sender Liability +X, beneficiary AR +X) until v10.0.28 adds settlement-driven clearing JE: `DR Customer Liability(sender) / CR Payee AR(beneficiary)`. The settle wizard already creates `remittance.tx.settlement` link records — v10.0.28 will hang the clearing JE off that link. Sister to the v9-era `bank_eur_out_usd_in` JE math fix (pending since April). Both should be discussed in the same Suleman accountant call.
- Canonical facts promoted to Unity: [[Remittance — Salueman Arif]] (bumped v10.0.25 → v10.0.27, hawala posting convention live on both prod DBs, Customer Liability account 489/210100 confirmed configured, sender's partner balance now reflects deposit).
