- **Recovery (v10.0.25)** — used GitHub HEAD `0ef5a90` (engrmuhammadamirnazir/remittance_management) as canonical source. cp-rn'd 84 missing files into local. Stripped CRLF→LF in the copies via `sed -i 's/\r$//'`. Added Dashboard menu (sequence 5) + Daily Console menu (sequence 7) + Money Flow grouping (sequence 10, parent of Flows / Transactions / Quick Create / Invoices) + Partners group (sequence 30, parent of All Partners + Authorised Beneficiaries) in `views/remittance_menus.xml`. Bumped to v19.0.10.0.25, deployed both DBs (atomic-swap, `-u remittance_management`, both `installed | 19.0.10.0.25`), HTTP 200 confirmed.
- **CRITICAL gotcha caught: `sed -i 's/\r$//'` corrupted `static/description/icon.png`** — stripped the 0x0D byte from the PNG signature `89 50 4E 47 0D 0A 1A 0A`, the IHDR header then decoded as 65536x65544 dimensions. App icon vanished from Odoo apps screen and menu sidebar. Restored byte-correct icon (10,273 bytes, 256x256, valid PNG) from prod tarball. Added `.gitattributes` permanently locking `*.png` `*.jpg` `*.svg` `*.woff*` `*.ttf` `*.pdf` `*.zip` `*.xlsx` `*.docx` `*.mp4` `*.mp3` `*.dump` `*.tar` `*.gz` as binary; source files (`.py` `.xml` `.js` `.scss` `.csv` `.md`) tagged `text eol=lf` for cross-platform consistency. Pattern reusable for any Windows-checkout repo with binary assets.
- **GitHub `engrmuhammadamirnazir/remittance_management` `0ef5a90..d4186fe` + tag `v19.0.10.0.25`** (2 commits: feat menu restore + icon-bytes fix). NO AI attribution. Local D:/Development monorepo: 3 new commits `ea034665e..f0681e785b` (v10.0.24 + v10.0.25 recovery + EcosireSolutions mirror sync). EcosireSolutions/Remittance-Management/remittance_management/ now matches GitHub HEAD content exactly. Pre-deploy backups taken on prod (`/tmp/pre_v10_0_25_remtest_20260502_065618.dump` 6.4MB sha `9ffe678a4e7d…` + `/tmp/pre_v10_0_25_remittanceaccounting_20260502_065618.dump` 6.2MB sha `a03a38e89d44…`).
- **Repo consolidation COMPLETE** — 178 leftover `worktree-agent-*` worktree dirs from today's parallel SDD work batch-deleted via `rm -rf .claude/worktrees`. All 178 stale `.git/worktrees/` metadata refs force-pruned. All 178 corresponding `worktree-agent-*` branch refs deleted via `git branch -D` (all subsumed by feat HEAD, no unmerged work). 3 stashes (`pre-rebase mirror snapshot` / `pre-rebase-v10-0-23-tracked-only` / `before-treasury-isolation`) dropped. Final state: **1 branch (`feat/v19.0.10-balances-and-ux`) + 1 worktree (main) + 0 stashes + 0 lock files**. Disk space recovered: ~10-15 GB from `.claude/worktrees/`.
- **Cross-project gotcha #1 — `sed -i` on a recursive copy corrupts binary files.** ALWAYS file-extension filter (`find ... -name '*.py' -o -name '*.xml' -o ...`) before line-ending normalisation, OR use `dos2unix` (detects binary headers and skips), OR add `.gitattributes` BEFORE the first commit on a new repo so git's autocrlf never touches binaries. Reusable in any cross-platform module recovery flow.
- **Cross-project gotcha #2 — Odoo 19 menu rewrites must preserve action-bound menuitems.** Any time `views/<module>_menus.xml` (or equivalent) is rewritten, audit BEFORE and AFTER for any `<menuitem action="...">` mapping to a registered `ir.actions.client` / `ir.actions.act_window` — orphaned actions become invisible UI features that survive on disk but have no entry point. Add to module-developer / module-validator audit checklist.
- **Cross-project gotcha #3 — `git filter-branch` on a multi-workspace monorepo can truncate sub-paths.** Today's AI-attribution strip dropped 84 files from `D:/Development/odoo19/server/addons/remittance_management/` while leaving `EcosireSolutions/Remittance-Management/remittance_management/` (in same monorepo) unaffected. Always verify file counts in EVERY workspace path after a filter-branch — diff against the upstream/canonical to catch drift before next commit.

- **NEW cross-project gotcha — Odoo XML-RPC `account.move.line.reconcile()` raises `Fault: cannot marshal None`** because Odoo's xmlrpc controller hardcodes `OdooMarshaller(allow_none=False)` for responses, but reconcile() returns dict containing None. Reconcile DOES succeed server-side. Wrap in try/except + verify by inspection (`matching_number`/`reconciled`/`amount_residual` read). Sister error: `Fault 2: 'You are trying to reconcile some entries that are already reconciled'` — different, means lines are in CLOSED matching chain; new line stays unmatched (cosmetic only if partner balance nets via offset). Pattern reusable in any Odoo XML-RPC client tool. Stored at `D:/Development/.../memory/feedback_xmlrpc_reconcile_marshalling_gotcha.md`.

Path consistent with Phase A 2026-05-01j convention.

The hotfix agents' mandatory test-install loop surfaced **8 distinct latent bugs total** — leroymerlin had 1 type / 60 occurrences (60× bare `@require_license()`); decathlon had **3 stacked bugs** that masked each other (locale Selection-vs-Char related-type / unsearchable-compute filter on `Datetime.now()`-dependent field / forward-reference menu parent); fnacdarty had **4 stacked bugs** (`_inherit` Monetary `currency_field`+ `related=` + `@api.depends` all referencing fields not on base model + literal `#` comment line in `ir.model.access.csv` causing cryptic `IndexError`). Always move `.OLD` OUT of addons-path. Sister to Bitnami dot-folder trap. Captured in `shared-knowledge/anti-patterns.md` so future deploys avoid it (decathlon + fnacdarty agents both successfully applied this gotcha after leroymerlin agent surfaced it).
- **Final Wave N state: 99/99 fleet at v19.0.2.x.0 / $499.** Demo HTTP 200 on all 5 subdomains: `carrefour.demo.ecosire.com` v0.0, `pccomponentes.demo.ecosire.com` v0.1, `leroymerlin/decathlon/fnacdarty.demo.ecosire.com` v0.2. ### 2026-05-02 — D:/Development (Suleman Remittance) — v10.0.8 NEW Partner Balance Detail drill-down + v10.0.9 XLSX 502 hotfix + v10.0.10 Dashboard xmlid hotfix
- **v10.0.8 NEW FEATURE LIVE both DBs.** Partner Balance Detail drill-down — click any partner row's "View Details" button in the Balances list → opens single-page OWL drill-down (`remittance_partner_balance_detail` client action) showing exactly *how* the final balance was reached + every associated transaction. Top bar (back-link, partner avatar, name + type pill, KYC + Sanctions pills, smart-action toolbar with Print Statement / Export XLSX / Export CSV / Partner Form / View Flows) + 3 hero balance cards EUR/USD/AED with positive/negative/zero color coding + In/Out totals + stats strip (Tx count / First Tx / Last Tx / Biggest Line clickable / Open Flows) + SVG running-balance line chart 3-currency layered last 6 months (no external dep) + Transaction Ledger table with running balance per currency, period chips (7d/30d/90d/YTD/All), currency tabs (All/EUR/USD/AED), each row clickable to source tx. Backed by single round-trip `remittance.partner.balance.get_breakdown(partner_id, period)` server method, multi-company aware via `env.companies`. Read-only.
- **v10.0.9 P0 hotfix:** XLSX/CSV downloads from the new Balance Detail returned 502 Proxy Error. Root cause: WSGI/werkzeug encodes HTTP headers as **latin-1**; em-dash (`—`, U+2014) in 3 XLSX builder titles crashed `Content-Disposition: filename="..."` mid-response with `UnicodeEncodeError`. Fix: em-dashes → hyphens in 3 builders + new `_safe_ascii_filename()` + `_rfc5987_filename()` helpers in `controllers/exports.py` emit dual `filename` + `filename*=UTF-8''…` directives per RFC 5987. Validated `curl XLSX → HTTP 200 6251 bytes Microsoft Excel 2007+`.
- **v10.0.10 P0 hotfix:** Dashboard alerts panel raised "Missing Action" — 3 broken xmlids in `models/remittance_dashboard.py`: `action_partner_remittance` → `action_partner_remittance_all`; `action_remittance_suspense_item` → `action_suspense`; `action_remittance_shipment` → `remittance_shipment_action`. Plus em-dash cleanup in 2 remaining XLSX builders (defensive — v10.0.9 sanitizer already caught them).
- **GitHub:** `engrmuhammadamirnazir/remittance_management` `main 675bef6..500b423..cd42724` + 3 new tags (v10.0.8 / v10.0.9 / v10.0.10) pushed. NO AI attribution. **9 release tags shipped today (v10.0.2 through v10.0.10).**
- **Cross-project pattern (1 new) — WSGI latin-1 Content-Disposition gotcha.** Any custom `Content-Disposition: filename="..."` header that includes a non-ASCII char (em-dash, smart quote, ellipsis, accented letter, CJK) crashes the response with UnicodeEncodeError → user sees 502 Proxy Error. Always sanitize via `_safe_ascii_filename()` AND emit RFC 5987 `filename*=UTF-8''…` fallback. Reusable in any Odoo workspace that builds custom HTTP file downloads (template at `D:/Development/odoo19/server/addons/remittance_management/controllers/exports.py`).
- **Pending for next session (carried):** v10.0.11 = `bank_eur_out_usd_in` JE math fix (still needs Suleman accountant call) + install-time `_check_xmlids` validator to catch broken `action_xmlid` references at install time instead of waiting for a user click.
- **Canonical facts promoted to Unity:** [[02 - Projects/Active Clients/Remittance (Suleman Arif)/README]] — module version `v10.0.7` → `v10.0.10`, frontmatter retained `updated: 2026-05-02`, full v10.0.8 Balance Detail feature documented + v10.0.9 + v10.0.10 hotfix sections added.

One stuck line forces SO header to `invoice_status='no'`, making real billed orders look non-billable. Default `'order'` on every service product setup. Saved as `feedback_service_products_invoice_policy_delivery_pitfall.md`.

### 2026-05-01 — D:/Development — Obliq MRP "phantom finished goods" bug diagnosed + patched + 22,622 raw moves backfilled silently
- Investigation of "Feb-Apr 2026 MOs cancelled" (Ziad concern via Amir) revealed deeper truth: MOs are state=done but their child raw_material `stock_move`s were CANCELLED with `picked=false, quantity=0`. From 2025-12 to 2026-05: 22,622 raw moves cancelled while 1,964 finished moves went done — **~2,541 furniture units produced from thin air with no raw material consumption**. AED 861,798 of cost flow missing.
- **Root cause**: `obliq_automation/models/auto_manufacturing.py:50-58` — `_auto_produce_mo()` set `move.quantity = product_uom_qty` but NOT `move.picked = True`. Sister method `_auto_close_mo()` already had `picked=True` on line 68 — the to-close path always worked. In Odoo 19, `mrp.production.button_mark_done()` cancels raw moves with `picked=false` instead of consuming. **Hard rule for fleet** (Sahara, Diamond, Future Vision Waredat, any client running v19 custom MRP automation): captured in `~/.claude/projects/D--Development/memory/feedback_odoo19_mrp_move_picked_required.md`. Detection probe ships in the same file.
- **Forward fix** (`obliq_automation` v19.0.7.0.0 → v19.0.8.0.0 → v19.0.8.1.0): added 1-line `move.picked = True`. v19.0.8.0.0 also added new **Manufacturing → Reporting → Raw Material Monthly Usage** dashboard tile (OWL component, Chart.js dual-axis, top-100 raw-material table, date filter, 1-click 4-sheet xlsx export at `/obliq/raw_material_usage/export`). Cron 80 disabled → patched module deployed → savepoint test verified (BOM 6957 STRUCTURE-C1, 20 components all DONE picked=True) → cron re-enabled.
- **Backfill executed silently** via direct SQL after discovering `stock_valuation_layer` table doesn't exist in Odoo 19 (replaced by `stock_avco_report` VIEW backed by `stock_move.value/is_in/is_out` columns directly). Single transaction touched: 22,622 stock_move UPDATEs (state=done, picked=true, quantity, value, is_out=true) + 22,622 stock_move_line INSERTs + stock_quant updates (215 src + 71 src-insert + 177 dest + 109 dest-insert) + 1,964 finished-move stock_move.value UPDATEs (0 → cost flow). Verification: 0 cancelled in scope, 0 picked=false, totals balance AED 861,793 raw OUT vs 861,798 finished IN within 5 AED rounding. Backup `obliq_pre_mrp_backfill_2026-04-30_191045.dump` (sha256 ebc23122, 19.6 MB) on Hetzner SB before commit.
- Same session also closed Kamal's earlier asks on prod: 220 orphan ADCB BSLs wiped (failed Apr stmt upload), Landmark 191 supplier_rank reset, 28 cancelled-as-valid bills flipped across 4 suppliers (took 6 iterations 1A-1F due to twin-detection conflicts), BC.006 wiped Option A (103 moves, balance 431,798→0, BC.001 went -20,737 needs Kamal decision). Detail in project-local `session_2026_04_30_obliq_kamal_completion.md` + `session_2026_05_01_obliq_mrp_backfill.md`.
- **Cross-project impact**: the picked=True rule applies fleet-wide to any v19 custom MRP automation — fleet sweep recommended (`grep -rn "button_mark_done\|move_raw_ids" --include="*.py"` and check each call site for `picked=True` next to quantity set). Direct-SQL backfill pattern reusable for any inventory cost-flow restoration where ORM `_action_done()` insufficient. Also: **Odoo 19 stock_valuation_layer is now a VIEW**, AVCO data lives on stock_move directly (`value`, `is_in`, `is_out` columns) — useful for any agent doing inventory data correction in v19.

### 2026-04-30 — D:/ECOSIRE.AI — Bulk PC-game drafts v2 — +115 published (139→254/2000); subscription-limit gap in generator surfaced and recovered manually
- **What ran:** Resumed `bulk-pc-game-drafts-v2` branch on `freepcgames.org` + `pcgamestore.net`. Block 2 (pcgs) closed clean: 93 successes / 7 failures / 13 banned-word retries. Block 3 (freepc) launched and reached 22 successes before 56 consecutive `unhandled: Exception: Command failed with exit code 1` rows pushed the run past the 10-failure auto-abort threshold. Final ledger: freepc 143 DONE / 1 FAILED / 56 PENDING; pcgs 111 DONE / 9 FAILED / 80 PENDING. **Total drafts: 254/2000.**
- **Root cause:** When the Claude Code Max 5-hour rolling window exhausts mid-run, `claude-agent-sdk` subprocess returns generic exit-code-1 with no usable stderr — generator's `SubscriptionLimitError` string-match detector never fires for this signature, blanket `except Exception` in the runner permanently FAILS the row. 56 articles erased into FAILED state from a single bad window. Recovered via SQL: `UPDATE article_jobs SET status='PENDING', last_error=NULL, attempts=0 WHERE status='FAILED' AND last_error LIKE 'unhandled: Exception: Command failed with exit code 1%'`.
- **Hardening pattern documented** in [[feedback_claude_agent_sdk_subscription]] (project-local): `_ConsecutiveExitOneTracker` — N≥3 exit-code-1s within 60s → raise `SubscriptionLimitError` instead of marking each row FAILED. Recommended to wire BEFORE any future >50-article subscription-mode batch.
- **Cross-project impact:** The exit-code-1 cascade signature applies to ANY workspace running batch generation against `claude-agent-sdk` on Max-subscription auth (D:/Development, EcosireClients, ECOSIRE.AI). The recovery SQL + tracker pattern are reusable. Pace observed: ~3-5 min/article across both blocks.
- **Resume tomorrow:** subscription window must reset first. Cmd: `cd ai-content-engine && python -m scripts.bulk_pc_game_drafts_v2.run --full < /dev/null 2>&1 | tee -a scripts/bulk_pc_game_drafts_v2/run.log`. Runner alternation lands on freepcgames.org (block_num 254//100=2 → +1=3 → odd → SITES[0]).
- **Canonical facts promoted to Unity:** none new — sites + plugin already inventoried.

### 2026-04-30 — D:/ECOSIRE.COM — Four-bug rescue: dashboard/projects 500, lockout-everyone, contacts auto-link, observability black hole
- `/dashboard/projects` "Internal Server Error" had a layered cause across web + api: React 19 hooks-after-early-return on the page (caused client crash → `error.tsx`), AND silent 500s from the API behind a `GlobalExceptionFilter` that only sent 5xx to Sentry (DSN unset → black hole). Filter now logs every 5xx with stack to console (commit `002d5e88`). Surfaced `column "privacy_visibility" does not exist` — schema drift on `projects` table (missing 3 cols: `privacy_visibility`, `alias_email`, `task_properties_definition`); fixed via direct ALTER + migration `0007`. **Pattern lesson: never let an exception filter fail silently — always Logger.error stack to PM2 for any status ≥ 500.**
- Sign-in 429 "lockout-everyone" bug: NestJS-on-Express had no `trust proxy` set, so every request resolved to `req.ip = 127.0.0.1` and the rate-limit (10 fails/15min) bucketed all users into one shared key — a few bad attempts locked everyone out. Fix: `app.getHttpAdapter().getInstance().set('trust proxy', 'loopback')` in `apps/api/src/main.ts`. **Pattern lesson: any NestJS app behind Nginx/Cloudflare on the same host MUST set trust proxy before rate-limit middleware runs — applies to every API across the fleet.**
- CRM lead → Contact auto-link wired: leads now create-or-link a contact at capture time (dedupe by email; falls back to phone). Backfilled 9 of 18 existing leads → contacts went 3 → 12. Backfill script needed manual UUID gen because raw postgres-js bypasses Drizzle `$defaultFn`.
- **Deploy script aborted twice mid-run** on Step 5 git-pull because PowerShell-via-Git-Bash treats SSH stderr as fatal NativeCommandError; both times maintenance flag was left ON until manually removed. 4th recurrence — **applies to every workspace deploying via Windows + scripts/deploy-production.sh.**
- Cross-project impact: trust-proxy + exception-filter-logging patterns must be applied to brand backends `api-odovation` and `api-muhammadamir` next time they're touched (still vulnerable). Deploy-script Windows bug affects every workspace using the same pattern.

### 2026-04-29 — D:/Development — Soovah/Quicken Wayfair connector — 1,470 missing POs RECOVERED to prod; v3.12.0 + v3.12.1 shipped fleet-wide
- **Trigger:** Quicken Accounting team sent Excel "2026 Sales Orders not imported to Odoo.xlsx" listing 1,471 rows / 1,470 unique CS- and CA-prefix POs spanning **Feb 19 – Apr 2 2026** that had never landed in their `soovah1` Odoo DB. Production server: `odoo.soovah.com` / `5.78.207.108` (Docker Odoo 19, Wayfair `wayfair_store_management` v19.0.3.11.0).
- **Root cause** in `import_orders_from_wayfair`: 3 cooperating bugs — `instance.last_sync = fields.Datetime.now()` set unconditionally + `MAX_PER_RUN = 200` cap + Dropship POs appended BEFORE CastleGate within batch loop. On any high-volume run, CastleGate POs got sliced off by the cap and `last_sync` rolled forward to NOW so the truncated tail was permanently abandoned.
- **Shipped v19/v18/v17.0.3.12.0** (5 fixes): CastleGate fetched first within batch loop; `po_data` sorted oldest-first by `poDate` before truncation; `last_sync` only advances on non-truncated runs; CastleGate fetch failures now create visible `wayfair.log` rows (was silent `_logger.warning`); `MAX_PER_RUN` raised 200→500; manual sync wizard's `date_from` field now wired through new `override_from_date` parameter; 6-test idempotency regression suite added. Pushed to `github.com/ecosire/wayfair_store_management` on main + 19.0 + 18.0 + 17.0 branches with v19/v18/v17.0.3.12.0 tags.
- **Recovery on prod:** pre-deploy pg_dump 54.6 MB → 3-way backup (local + Dropbox-synced folder + Soovah `/tmp`); SFTP'd 6 module files via paramiko + `docker restart odoo-one-odoo19-1`; HTTP 200 + manifest verified. Paused all 17 Wayfair scheduled actions. Ran 9 import passes via `docker exec -i odoo shell --db_host=db --db_port=5432 --db_user=odoo --db_password=odoo19@2025 -d soovah1 << "PYEOF"` calling `import_orders_from_wayfair(inst, override_from_date=DATE)` with stride covering Feb 15 + Mar 12/17/22/27 + Apr 1/6 — drained **782 NEW mappings**.
- **Found additional bug + shipped v3.12.1 hot-fix same day:** `sale.order.date_order` was being reset to NOW for newly imported orders. Cause: `auto_validate_delivery`'s `picking.button_validate()` triggers downstream stock compute methods that re-overwrite the in-code `odoo_order.write({'date_order': po_date})` workaround inside `_apply_instance_auto_workflow`. Fix: appended a final `cr.execute("UPDATE sale_order SET date_order=%s WHERE id=%s") + invalidate_recordset(['date_order'])` block AFTER the existing try/except — direct SQL bypasses ORM compute/inverse triggers entirely. Backported, published to all 4 GitHub branches, deployed to Soovah. **GL accounting was correct throughout** (`account.move.invoice_date` and `account.move.date` always pinned correctly during import); v3.12.1 only fixes the cosmetic `date_order` field on `sale.order`.
- **Final result on prod:** **1,470/1,470 Excel POs recovered (100%)**. Invoices distributed correctly across original PO months: Feb 295, Mar 1,114, Apr 62 — all `posted` with correct `invoice_date`. 817 sale.order `date_order` records back-corrected mid-recovery via SQL UPDATE driven by parsed `'PO X date_order will be Y'` lines from `/opt/odoo-one/etc/odoo-server.log` (1,520 lines parsed). All 17 Wayfair crons re-enabled post-recovery.
- **Cross-project impact:** v3.12.0 + v3.12.1 patches are fleet-wide for the Wayfair Store Management module — every App Store customer running v3.11.0 or earlier is exposed to the same backlog-stranding bug. Recovery procedure documented in `D:/Development/EcosireClients/ProspectiveClients/Soovah-Wayfair/RECOVERY_v19.0.3.12.0.md` + `RECOVERY_RESULT.md` for any other affected customer. **Fleet sweep recommended** — other `*_store_management` modules with the clone-from-Shopify lineage may share the same `last_sync = fields.Datetime.now()` + `MAX_PER_RUN` truncation pattern; grep + patch each like Wayfair did. Reusable agent gotchas captured: docker-compose `odoo shell` socket failure (need explicit `--db_host=db` flags), windowed-pagination `override_from_date` advance is fragile when API returns mixed-date streams (use fixed N-day stride per pass instead of MAX-of-recent), `action_confirm` + `auto_validate_delivery` interaction in Odoo 19 (direct SQL the only reliable date_order pin).
- **Canonical facts promoted to Unity:** [[Ecosire - Production Servers]] (Quicken row updated to v19.0.3.12.1 + 1,470-PO recovery note); [[Ecosire - Client Portfolio]] (Quicken status updated); [[Server & Key Inventory]] (Quicken row module version updated). New cross-project feedback note: `feedback_storagebox_bx11_password_stale.md` (Hetzner Storage Box BX11 password in Unity is stale — auth rejects, must reset via Hetzner Robot UI; ad-hoc backups go to Dropbox-synced folder until then).

Documented live SDK message shape (`AssistantMessage.content[].text`, `ResultMessage.result`) plus transient-error retry pattern (subprocess startup timeouts after ~50 sequential calls — needs 45s sleep + single retry).

- **Cross-project impact:** `feedback_claude_agent_sdk_subscription` rule applies to any future ECOSIRE.AI / EcosireClients / Development workspace task that needs sustained Claude generation without burning Anthropic credits. Reference impl: `D:\ECOSIRE.AI\ai-content-engine\scripts\bulk_pc_game_drafts_v2\generator.py`.

### 2026-04-26 — D:/Development — Suleman Remittance v19.0.10.0.0 LIVE on prod+remtest + 4 fleet-wide Odoo 19 P0 patterns captured
- **Suleman Remittance v10 LIVE on prod (`remittanceaccounting.ecosire.com`) + remtest (`remtest.ecosire.com`)** in a single end-to-end session: Balances dashboard restored (lost in v9), smart-default sweep (currency auto-locks from `kind`, location auto-fills from partner), Compliance Matrix wired with real `ValidationError` teeth (v9 `_check_required` was DEFINED-but-NEVER-CALLED orphan), 17 PDF/XLSX/CSV reports under new `Remittance → Reports` menu, PKR currency removed (3 rows from `res_company_activated_currency_rel`), audit fixes A2 (partner balance from GL not `tx.amount`) + A3 (`balance.line.role` from `is_remittance_intermediary` flag). 53 commits on `feat/v19.0.10-balances-and-ux`; GitHub `engrmuhammadamirnazir/remittance_management` main fast-forwarded `395ded3..11a7e1b` + tag `v19.0.10.0.0` published. Pre-deploy backups stamped `20260426_195210` on server. User Manual addendum PDF (245 KB, 5 pages, Ecosire letterhead) at `D:/EcosireClients/ActiveClients/Suleman-Remittance/docs/Remittance_User_Manual_v19.0.10.0.0_Addendum.pdf`.
- **4 fleet-wide Odoo 19 P0 patterns captured** as project-local feedback files (apply to ANY future Odoo 19 module work):
    1. **RelaxNG strictness on data files** — Odoo 19's `import_xml.rng` rejects `<odoo noupdate="1">` with direct `<record>` children (wrap in `<data noupdate="1">`) AND rejects `<![CDATA[]]>` inside `<field type="html">` (use inline HTML). Bisect technique via `lxml.etree.RelaxNG.validate()` per-record documented.
    2. **`web.external_layout_standard` inheritance trap** — v19 parent uses `t-attf-class="header ..."` (compile-time attribute), so `xpath //div[hasclass('header')]` cannot locate the element. Write self-contained primary template with `<t t-out="0"/>` slot instead of inheriting.
    3. **🔥 P0 trap — `<t t-inherit="web.ListView" t-inherit-mode="primary">` with broken xpath** — corrupts list-view rendering FLEET-WIDE (every list view in the UI throws OwlError, not just the one that registered the inheritance). Caught BY THE USER on prod within minutes of deploy. Hotfix: delete inheriting template + registry entry + js_class. Recommended pattern: wrapper Component embedding `<View>` as child OR kanban-header pattern.
    4. **Bitnami Odoo 19 CLI environment** — `pg_dump`/`psql` at `/opt/bitnami/postgresql/bin/`; CLI requires `LD_LIBRARY_PATH=/opt/bitnami/postgresql/lib:/opt/bitnami/common/lib` or psycopg2 fails on `libpq.so.5`; default log level is WARNING so silent successful upgrades; canonical log at `/opt/bitnami/odoo/log/odoo-server.log`.
- **Cross-project impact:** the 4 patterns above are fleet-wide — every Ecosire Odoo 19 module (215 modules across `D:/Development/odoo19/server/addons/` and the 7 active client tenant repos) will benefit. Unity stays focused on cross-workspace canonical entities; the patterns live in project-local `D:/Development/.claude/projects/D--Development/memory/feedback_*.md` because that's where Odoo-19-specific learnings belong (and where module-developer / odoo-engineer agents read them on every task).
- **Canonical facts promoted to Unity:** [[Suleman Arif - Remittance]] client status updated (v10 LIVE, both DBs at `19.0.10.0.0`, GitHub tag `v19.0.10.0.0`, User Manual PDF delivered, KPI hero banner deferred to v10.0.x patch).

### 2026-04-26 — D:/Development — Oenoteca Enohance 86/2026 PO end-to-end on prod + Odoo 19 product-category gotcha captured
- **Routine inventory entry on Oenoteca prod (Hetzner 23.88.13.113):** Enohance 86/2026 (EUR 11,737.75, 75 bottles, 21 Library wines) entered as **PO P00168 → WH/IN/00123 → BILL/2026/04/0008 → LC/2026/0027 → JE STJ/2026/04/0011**. Tariff 15% via canonical formula (EUR × 0.15 × 1.20 = $2,112.79) + **freight $12/btl one-time exception** (75 × $12 = $900, vs standard $8/btl) = LC USD $3,012.79. All 21 new products (IDs 1719-1739) routed to **500004 THE LIBRARY COGS** per user instruction.
- **Cross-project pattern — Odoo 19 product-creation gotcha (worth fleet-wide knowledge):** new `product.product` created via XML-RPC without explicit `categ_id` defaults to `cost_method='standard'` + `valuation='periodic'`, which **silently breaks landed-cost computation** ("Landed costs can only be applied for products with FIFO or average costing method"). Error surfaces on the LC step, not on product create — easy to misdiagnose. Recovery path validated 2026-04-26: assign correct categ_id mid-pipeline, then re-run `compute_landed_cost` — succeeds because Odoo derives valuation_adjustment from `move.price_unit × quantity`, not from missing prior SVL state. Captured as fleet feedback `D:/Development/.../memory/feedback_odoo19_new_product_categ_default.md`. Applies to any agent creating products via XML-RPC against any Odoo 19 instance with landed costs (Oenoteca, future inventory-heavy clients with Italian/imported flows).
- **Operational nits surfaced:** (a) `product.product.create()` returns LIST `[id]` not scalar via XML-RPC `execute_kw('create', [vals])` — must unwrap; (b) `stock.valuation.layer` model NOT exposed via XML-RPC on this build; (c) Windows console cp1252 chokes on Unicode arrows (`→`) — use `PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8` or stick to ASCII.
- **Wine-taxonomy gap re-confirmed (Oenoteca-local):** `Red Wine Spain OOSHW` category does not exist (memory flagged 2026-04-17 for Vega Sicilia Valbuena 2015). Today's Vega Sicilia Unico 2005 + 2011 (both 14%) parked in OOSLW; reclass pending.
- **Cross-project impact:** the Odoo 19 categ_id gotcha is fleet-wide. No new canonical facts (no clients/servers/credentials/prices/modules). No sibling workspace touched.
- **Canonical facts promoted to Unity:** none — gotcha lives in D:/Development project-local feedback file (which is the right place for fleet-wide Odoo patterns; Unity stays focused on cross-workspace canonical entities).

Both on ECOSIRE letterhead, unsigned per fleet rule for user guides. Generators reusable at `D:/EcosireClients/ActiveClients/Obliq/internal/generate_{bank_upload_sop,kamal_handoff}.py`.
- **Cross-project impact (fleet-wide lesson for ALL client-facing PDF generators):** reportlab `Table` cells with long text OR HTML entities (`&quot;` `&amp;` `&rarr;` etc.) MUST be wrapped in `Paragraph(text, style)`. Plain strings do NOT word-wrap AND do NOT decode entities — they overflow into sibling cells AND render entities literally. First version of Kamal handoff PDF shipped with 5 corrupted tables; user caught immediately. Fix: `_p()` helper + `_wrap_rows()` sweep that Paragraph-wraps every cell before passing to `Table()`. Applies across Diamond, Sahara, Oenoteca, Remittance, Alvi, Amalfi, Quicken, and all future client generators. Diamond's `generate_m2_user_guide.py` is the canonical reference (already does it right).
- **Cross-project impact (lesson on audit scripts):** three of my seven audit findings were false positives because the audit matched on text substrings / loose (date, amount) tuples without triangulation. Domain specialists (accountant, database-engineer, functional-consultant) triangulated each from 3 independent sources (file / DB / counter-account) and disproved them. Saved ~8 hours of wasted reversal work. Pattern: always triangulate before concluding on accounting data; a text-search audit is a candidate-finder, not a verdict.

### 2026-04-24 — D:/Development — Sulaman Standard: new vanilla Odoo 19 DB on Sahara's shared Bitnami (3rd subdomain on the same box)
- Provisioned `suleman` DB on the existing AWS Bitnami at 3.232.201.222 — live at https://suleman.ecosire.com (Cloudflare orange-cloud, LE cert SAN expanded sahara→sahara+testing+suleman, expiry 2026-07-23). Admin = `sulearifuae@gmail.com` (same Suleman Arif as the Remittance client + Sahara CEO contact, password matched to Sahara admin per user instruction). Apps installed via XML-RPC: sales / purchase / account_accountant / stock / crm / hr / project / contacts / mail / website / l10n_ae (UAE/AED/Asia-Dubai). DB created via POST `/web/database/create` with master_pwd. New client folder `D:/EcosireClients/ActiveClients/Sulaman-Standard/` with CLAUDE.md + reusable `scripts/install_apps.py` + `scripts/verify_public.py`.
- **Cross-project impact (reusable patterns for any Bitnami Odoo box on this fleet):**
  1. **Catch-all-vhost trick** — Bitnami's stock `odoo-https-vhost.conf` uses `ServerAlias *` and Odoo's `dbfilter = ^%d$` does the rest. Adding a new tenant subdomain to ANY existing Bitnami Odoo (Sahara / Remittance / Wayfair-on-Quicken-style boxes) requires ONLY (a) DNS to origin + (b) `certbot certonly --standalone --expand` to add the SAN. No per-DB vhost file, no `Include` shuffles, no `a2ensite`. Pattern works behind Cloudflare orange-cloud — re-confirms the 2026-04-24 ADNET finding that LE HTTP-01 succeeds through CF Full-Strict without DNS-01.
  2. **Master-password URL-encoding gotcha** — `r04uU1E+gekv` contains `+`, which curl form-encodes as a literal space. Use `--data-urlencode` (not raw `-d`) when scripting `/web/database/create`. A typo (`gekV` capital V) returns HTTP 200 with the DB-manager HTML re-rendered (no error JSON), which can be misread as success. Watch the Odoo log for `Registry changed, signaling through the database` to confirm actual creation.
  3. **/web/database/list returns `[]` from localhost** when `dbfilter=^%d$` is in play — the regex fails on `Host: 127.0.0.1`. Don't interpret empty list as "creation failed"; query Postgres directly or hit the endpoint with a matching Host header.
- **Cross-project impact (entity):** Suleman Arif now has THREE Odoo systems on two different servers — Sahara PMS (`saharaproperties` + `testingsahara` on 3.232.201.222) for property work, Remittance (`remittanceaccounting` + `remtest` on 52.28.45.137) for the European remittance entity, and now this vanilla `suleman` DB on the Sahara box for general/personal use. Future agents asking "where's Suleman's data?" should disambiguate by use case before SSH-ing.
- **Canonical facts promoted to Unity:** [[Ecosire - Production Servers]] — Server 3 row updated (3 SANs on cert, 3 DBs on box, catch-all-vhost trick documented).

### 2026-04-24 — D:/Ad Network Website — ADNET prod seeded with 4 role-spanning demo accounts (admin + ops + advertiser + publisher)
- **Problem surfaced:** the flagship `adsnetwork.ecosire.com` admin row was unusable — `pnpm db:seed` (`packages/db/src/seed.ts`) deliberately writes a `$seed$`-prefixed sentinel into `users.password_hash` and `verifyPassword()` short-circuits to `false` on that prefix. Intended flow is password reset via email, but no SMTP is wired in prod yet. Resolved by SSH-ing in with `adsnetwork.pem`, bcrypt-hashing a 16-char `base64url` secret using the repo's own `bcrypt@5.1.1` + `postgres@3.4.9` resolved from `node_modules/.pnpm/` (pnpm doesn't hoist, so direct `require("bcrypt")` at the app root fails with `MODULE_NOT_FOUND`), and running a single `UPDATE users SET password_hash=$1` + `DELETE FROM sessions WHERE user_id=$1` against `$DATABASE_URL` from `/opt/adsnetwork/app/.env.production`. Verified round-trip with `bcrypt.compare`; hash prefix now `$2b$` length 60, 0 stray sessions. Then inserted 3 more rows (advertiser + publisher + ops) with `ON CONFLICT (organization_id, email_lower) DO UPDATE` so the script is idempotent.
- **Preloaded state so the dashboards aren't empty:** advertiser has `kyc_status=approved` + `balance_cents=5_000_000` ($50k, bypasses Stripe funding), publisher has `application_status=approved` + `kyc_status=approved` + `trust_score=90` + `conversions_quarantine_remaining=0` (R7 quarantine disabled). Org ID `b435a73d-2bf4-4198-b22a-edcdb186317b`, deploy dir `/opt/adsnetwork/app`, PM2 runs 8 processes (web, api, tracking, 5 workers). Credential values are in the active Claude transcript only — not promoted to Unity and should be treated burn-after-use; after first login the operator should change them via the settings UI.
- **Cross-project impact — 2 whitelabel-clone gotchas worth fleet-wide awareness:**
  1. **The `$seed$` sentinel first-deploy trap.** Any clone using `@adnet/db` seed (every future ADNET whitelabel client) will have the same unusable admin row on first deploy. `packages/auth-core/src/services/password.service.ts` expects SMTP to be configured so the `POST /auth/password/reset-request` flow can deliver the token. Until SMTP is wired, operators must either (a) run a direct-DB bcrypt UPDATE (the recipe in this session), or (b) pre-configure Resend/SES in `.env.production` before running `pnpm tenant:provision`. Candidate fix for the seed: accept an `ADNET_SEED_ADMIN_PASSWORD` env var and, if set, write a real bcrypt hash so the operator can log in immediately. Worth flagging in `whitelabel-clone` skill's bootstrap checklist.
  2. **pnpm workspace + native-addon resolution from ad-hoc node scripts.** `node -e 'require("bcrypt")'` run from the app root fails with `MODULE_NOT_FOUND` on any pnpm-installed `node_modules` because pnpm doesn't hoist unless the calling package declares the dep. Workaround: `require("/opt/adsnetwork/app/node_modules/.pnpm/bcrypt@5.1.1/node_modules/bcrypt")`. Same gotcha applies to any SSH-in-and-patch workflow on D:/ECOSIRE.COM, D:/ECOSIRE.IO, D:/ECOSIRE.AI (all pnpm monorepos). Cleaner fix for future runbooks: write the script as a file inside `apps/api` where the dep is declared, then `pnpm --filter @adnet/api exec node script.mjs`.
- **Canonical facts promoted to Unity:** none. [[MOC - Hive Mind]] already has ADNET at row 8 and the EC2 entry (`50.16.169.132` / `D:\Ad Network Website\adsnetwork.pem`) at the server inventory; nothing new to add. Demo-account values are *not* written to `03 - Areas/Credentials & Access/` — they're meant to be rotated on first login.

### 2026-04-24 — D:/ECOSIRE.COM — P0 outage fix + CI/CD regression-prevention suite (6 commits, all live on prod)
- **Incident:** every `/products/[slug]` page was rendering the generic "Something went wrong" error boundary because the server component referenced `odooVersions` (undefined in scope; correct name in that file is `ldOdooVersions`). Introduced by commit `bd07e063` when the SEO/JSON-LD expansion renamed the local but missed this one usage in the visually-hidden LLM summary. Impact: ~215 product pages dead → SEO/conversion/revenue hit.
- **Root-cause analysis revealed the CI/CD pipeline was the actual failure.** `Lint & Typecheck` CI had been flagging `TS2552: Cannot find name 'odooVersions'` for multiple commits, but the deploy path had four silent bypasses stacked: (1) `apps/web/next.config.ts` had `typescript.ignoreBuildErrors: true` (legacy t3.large OOM workaround — server is on t3.xlarge now), (2) `scripts/pre-deploy-check.sh` only ran `next build` (which ignores TS with that flag) not a standalone typecheck, (3) `scripts/deploy-production.sh` never queried `gh run list` to verify CI status before deploying, (4) 22/30 recent CI runs were red and everyone kept stacking commits on top. Plus 8 standing `ToolEmailGate` TS errors were masking new errors in CI output.
- **Prevention suite shipped (commits `19614637` → `8eeb8062`):** Step 0 CI-status gate in `deploy-production.sh` (refuses deploy unless `gh run list --branch=main --workflow=ci.yml` conclusion=success; override `DEPLOY_SKIP_CI=1` for emergencies with visible warning). `next.config.ts` `ignoreBuildErrors` flipped to `false`. `pre-deploy-check.sh` grew a `pnpm turbo typecheck` Step 5/7. `.githooks/pre-commit` now runs `tsc --noEmit` on apps/web when staged files include `apps/web/**/*.{ts,tsx}`. `tests/public/product-detail.spec.ts` (Playwright) hits 3 slugs + asserts zero error-boundary heading (env-independent primary assertion) + rich assertions when real product data is served. `.github/workflows/ci.yml` gains `notify-failure` job that posts to `SLACK_CI_WEBHOOK` secret on red main (no-op if secret absent). Coverage tooling added: `@vitest/coverage-v8`, widened `include: src/**/*.ts`, ratchet thresholds at current floor (lines/statements 25, functions 30, branches 50 — ratchet UP over time, never lowered without a recorded reason). Also fixed the long-flaky `auth-core/src/services/token.service.spec.ts` "rejects tampered tokens" test that mutated only the last base64url char (sometimes flipped only spare/unused bits → verify legitimately returned true). E2E CI job timeout bumped 30→45min to stop spurious cancellations on the 19k-page static prebuild.
- **Cross-project impact — 3 patterns worth propagating fleet-wide:**
  1. **"CI gate on deploy" pattern.** Any workspace with a manual/script-driven deploy (D:/Development agent fleet, D:/ECOSIRE.AI, D:/ECOSIRE.IO, D:/EcosireClients/*) should audit its deploy script for "does this verify CI on HEAD is green before shipping?" Copy-paste the ~20-line `Step 0` block from `D:/ECOSIRE.COM/scripts/deploy-production.sh` (uses `gh run list --branch=main --workflow=<name> --limit=1 --json conclusion,status,headSha`). Same pattern flagged as a problem in ECOSIRE.IO's session above (Husky-free pre-commit hook); CI-status-gate is the natural deploy-time counterpart.
  2. **`ignoreBuildErrors: true` is a time bomb.** Any Next.js config in the fleet carrying that flag should be audited — CI-as-the-gate *only works if the deploy actually waits on CI*. Until that's true, the flag hides bugs. Same reasoning applies to `eslint.ignoreDuringBuilds` and Vite/SWC equivalents.
  3. **PowerShell-wrapped SSH trips bash `set -e` via the ERR trap** — documented pattern (already in ECOSIRE.COM memory as `feedback_powershell_ssh_scripts.md`). Recurred twice today at Step 5 (`git pull`) of `deploy-production.sh`: the pull ran successfully but the `NativeCommandError` wrapper stderr tripped the trap. Fleet-wide fix candidates: either (a) wrap `do_ssh()` output with `| Out-String` + explicit exit code, or (b) prefer native Git Bash SSH when available. Any workspace whose deploy script uses the same `do_ssh()` helper pattern (D:/ECOSIRE.COM, D:/Development, D:/ECOSIRE.AI, D:/ECOSIRE.IO, D:/Ad Network Website — all likely forked from the same template) will hit this. Worth a coordinated fix in one session.
- **Canonical facts promoted to Unity:** none. No new clients, servers, credentials, prices, modules, or URLs. All changes are code + CI config inside D:/ECOSIRE.COM; project-local memory in `~/.claude/projects/D--ECOSIRE-COM/memory/` captures the ECOSIRE-specific detail.

### 2026-04-24 — D:/ECOSIRE.IO — launch-ready platform upgrade: competitive research + AI SRE + full hardening (1 commit `da7eb59`, 135 files)
- **Single cohesive commit atop Phase D (f7a09d0)** that takes ECOSIRE.IO from code-complete to public-launch-ready. Executed as 3 parallel waves of 4 subagents each + security remediation: (Wave 1) nginx/systemd/scripts/CI-workflows/helmet/throttler/Sentry/CSP/HSTS, Husky-free pre-commit hook, Stripe seed+dunning+trial+tax, real cloud-credential validation, forgot/reset-password flow, 7 legal pages (ToS/Privacy/DPA/AUP/Cookies/Refund/Security) + security.txt, marketing pages + 3 competitor comparison pages (odoo-sh/Cloudpepper/Frappe), sitemap+robots+OG, DB schema additions (AuditLog, PasswordResetToken, AIInsight, PreviewEnvironment, NewsletterSubscriber, UsageEvent, ApiRateLimitEvent + dunning/trial fields + `Server.agentTokenHash`). (Wave 2) AI SRE engine (cost-advisor/anomaly-watcher/slow-query-detector/autoscale-predictor scheduled via BullMQ), per-PR preview envs with auto-sunset + GitHub webhook auto-destroy, web shell (PTY-over-WS with allowlisted unprivileged user), file manager with strict allowlist + realpath symlink-escape, 1-click migration importers from odoo.sh/Frappe-Cloud/Odoo-Online, metered billing via Stripe usage records, worker entry point, platform status endpoint, `@ecosire/cli`, `terraform-provider-ecosire` (Go), `apps/docs` MDX, observability stack (Prom+Grafana+Alertmanager+Loki+Promtail, 4 provisioned dashboards, 10 alert rules). (Wave 3) 20 API unit specs + 2 E2E + 5 Playwright smoke specs + 1 agent cross-cutting pytest. Security review found 3 Critical + 6 High; all 9 fixed in the same commit (agent-token bcrypt verification, GITHUB_WEBHOOK_SECRET mandatory, 2FA pending-token + throttle, OAuth code-exchange, refresh-guard correct strategy, agent systemd hardened with tight sudoers, SSRF guard on user-supplied dump URLs, PITR db_name shell-injection guard, WS-gateway origin allowlist).
- **Verification:** `pnpm --filter @ecosire/api build` clean (zero errors), `pnpm --filter @ecosire/web build` clean (48 routes static+dynamic, after resolving 2 issues: stale `@prisma/client` resolution fixed by pinning `^7.8.0` directly in apps/api/package.json, and Next.js 16 App Router rejecting `export const metadata` from `'use client'` pages — removed from 8 dashboard pages and wrapped 2 auth pages using `useSearchParams` in Suspense boundaries).
- **Cross-project impact — 9 fleet-wide reusable patterns shipped from this session:** (1) **Husky-free Git pre-commit hook** pattern (`.githooks/pre-commit` + `"prepare"` script setting `core.hooksPath`) — drop-in for every workspace on this machine; detects `.env`/AWS/Stripe/PEM/JWT secrets and runs scoped typecheck; the allow-template fix (`grep -vE '\.(example|sample|template|dist)$'`) is the non-obvious gotcha. (2) **Prisma 7 + pnpm workspace store double-version trap** — if an app imports `@prisma/client` directly without declaring it, pnpm may resolve to a stale pinned version from another package's lock entry; fix is to declare the client explicitly in the consuming app's `package.json` at the version matching the generator. (3) **Next.js 16 App Router prerender errors** — `export const metadata` is forbidden in `'use client'` pages; also any client page using `useSearchParams()` must be wrapped in `<Suspense>` or the production build fails during static export. (4) **Real cloud-credential validation** pattern for any multi-cloud control plane (Hetzner `GET /servers`, AWS STS `GetCallerIdentity` via native crypto SigV4 so no AWS SDK dep, DO `/v2/account`, Vultr `/v2/account`, OVH `/me`) with 5s timeout — reusable for D:/Development agent fleet provisioning, D:/ECOSIRE.AI tenant provisioning, D:/ECOSIRE.COM infrastructure. (5) **SSRF guard** for user-supplied URLs (scheme allowlist + `socket.getaddrinfo` + reject RFC-1918/127/169.254/::1/fc00::/7/fe80::/10 + TLS SNI with resolved IP to prevent DNS rebinding) — applies to any service that fetches customer-supplied URLs (ECOSIRE.AI import workflows, ECOSIRE.COM website crawler). (6) **Shell-metacharacter injection guard for DB-name in `archive_command`** — regex `^[a-zA-Z_][a-zA-Z0-9_]{0,62}$` + `os.path.realpath` allowlist for paths — pattern fits any script composing PG or nginx config from user input. (7) **Husky-free pre-commit + secret regex** set is now a baseline. (8) **Agent systemd hardening** template (NoNewPrivileges=true, ProtectSystem=strict, ReadWritePaths, no CAP_SETUID, sudoers fragment with NOPASSWD allowlist for systemctl/pg_dump/pg_restore/pg_basebackup/bench/nginx-t) — reusable for every agent deployed on client servers across Sahara/Obliq/Oenoteca/Quicken/Diamond/Alvi/Remittance/Amalfi fleet. (9) **Competitive "most advanced" wedge** — positioning as "the only ERP hosting with an AI SRE (cost advisor + anomaly + auto-scale + slow-query)" is reusable narrative for ECOSIRE.COM messaging and for any future pitch/proposal generators in D:/Development `scripts/client_docs/`.
- **Competitive facts captured from web research (for any future Ecosire pitch/content):** odoo.sh ~$57.60/worker + $0.20/GB + $18/staging + $38.90/user — Odoo-only, locked FS, no apt. Cloudpepper $29-$262 — Odoo-only, no AI, no multi-region, no public SLA. Frappe Cloud $5 shared → $1000 hybrid — ERPNext-only, marketplace delays. ECOSIRE.IO target white-label $149 (40% under Cloudpepper, 85% under Frappe hybrid). ### 2026-04-24 — D:/Ad Network Website — ADNET platform built end-to-end + deployed to adsnetwork.ecosire.com (new AWS server 50.16.169.132)
- **Zero to live in one session.** 215 files, 10K+ LOC across Turborepo monorepo (8 packages, 3 apps, 5 workers) forked from ECOSIRE.COM's proven NestJS 11 + Next.js 15 + Drizzle + PG16 + Redis 7 + Fastify 5 stack. Whitelabel from day 1 via root `tenant.config.ts` — any client clone needs only a fork, one file edit, and 5 `openssl rand -base64 32` rotations to launch under their own brand.
- **Deployed live** at https://adsnetwork.ecosire.com (new AWS EC2 `50.16.169.132`, Cloudflare proxied, Let's Encrypt HTTP-01 cert — works with CF Full-Strict). 8 PM2 processes (web, api, tracking, + 5 workers), Postgres 16 with 36 tables via `drizzle-kit push`, Redis 7 for BullMQ + sessions, Nginx with Cloudflare IP ranges + shared `/etc/nginx/adnet-proxy.conf` include. All 18 public routes return 200; API health reports db+redis green. Swagger live at `/docs`.
- **Cross-project impact (reusable patterns promoted fleet-wide):**
  1. **Whitelabel via root config + override file** — `tenant.config.ts` at repo root with deep-merge of optional `tenant.override.config.ts` (gitignored) lets client clones pull upstream forever without merge conflicts. Better than env vars because the config is typed + versioned with the code. Pattern applies to every SaaS-style workspace (ECOSIRE.IO already whitelabels Odoo hosting — candidate for the same approach).
  2. **Fastify 5 migrations** — `reply.redirect(url, code)` argument order flipped from v4. Any workspace on Fastify 4 upgrading needs the rewrite.
  3. **Let's Encrypt HTTP-01 works behind Cloudflare Full-Strict** with `certbot --nginx --no-redirect` — NO DNS-01 challenge needed. ISRG servers successfully fetch the ACME challenge through CF's proxy on port 80. This means any Cloudflare-proxied workspace can get a real origin cert without touching CF API keys. Applies to ECOSIRE.COM, ECOSIRE.IO, future clones.
  4. **Husky-free pre-commit hook** (from ECOSIRE.COM 2026-04-24) SHIPPED in the new repo from commit 1 — `.githooks/pre-commit` + `"prepare": "git config core.hooksPath .githooks"` in root package.json. Validates the pattern scales to fresh projects, not just retrofit.
  5. **Fleet TypeScript gotchas re-confirmed and logged:** (a) packages extending `config-tsconfig/node.json` inherit `types: ["node"]` — every such package MUST list `@types/node` in devDeps or add `types: []` override; (b) `import.meta.url` breaks in CommonJS packages even if tsc compiles — use `__dirname` for Node scripts; (c) NestJS ValidationPipe crashes at boot if `class-validator` isn't installed, even if you only use Zod — drop the global pipe entirely when using Zod; (d) Next.js 15 `useSearchParams()` in a `"use client"` page MUST be wrapped in Suspense or static prerender fails.
- **Canonical facts promoted to Unity:** [[MOC - Hive Mind]] (Ad Network Website row updated from "no code yet" → full stack deployed + server row added), [[Ecosire - Production Servers]] (if present — new 50.16.169.132 entry added if the note exists, otherwise referenced via MOC). New deploy key at `D:\Ad Network Website\adsnetwork.pem` — file path only, value never quoted; `.gitignore` now blocks `*.pem`/`*.key` repo-wide.
- **Open follow-ups** (documented in CLAUDE.md, not blocking): (1) Add `trk.adsnetwork.ecosire.com` grey-cloud DNS for MMPs that reject path-based tracking URLs (`/r/*` currently lives on main domain); (2) Cloudflare page rule "Cache Level: Bypass" on `/r/*` to prevent redirect caching; (3) Switch to Cloudflare Origin CA cert so LE rate limits don't apply long-term.

### 2026-04-24 — D:/ECOSIRE.COM — blog i18n hotfix + Husky-free pre-commit hook prevents 4th recurrence
- **Bug surfaced from screenshot.** `/blog` listing page 1/85 was rendering raw key paths (`blog.posts.power-bi-vs-tableau-2026.title` etc.) for 6 cards in every locale — the 6 newly-merged posts from the earlier `6dec0442` deploy shipped without their `blog.posts.{slug}.{title,description}` entries in `apps/web/messages/en.json`. Third recurrence (prior 2026-03-15, 2026-03-17). The pre-deploy / pre-push gate scripts (`scripts/pre-deploy-check.sh`, `scripts/pre-push-check.sh`) that catch this both *exist and pass* — but no one ran them, and there was no enforced Git pre-commit hook. Parallel-agent merges keep slipping past the manual gate.
- **Fix shipped at `a382a665`.** Ran `validate-blog-i18n.mjs --fix` (frontmatter → en.json), `translate-missing.mjs` (8 locales), `patch-hi-ur-missing.mjs` (hi/ur English fallback by convention), `fix-broken-icu-placeholders.mjs` (1 mangled `{var}` in pt). Validator now reports `1017 posts × 11 locales, all keys present, MDX-safe`. IndexNow: 16,258 URLs across 11 locales submitted.
- **Cross-project impact — reusable pattern for ALL workspaces.** The prevention is a **Husky-free Git hook** that any workspace on this machine can copy in 5 minutes: (1) ship `.githooks/pre-commit` checked into the repo (runs the relevant validator only when the trigger files are staged, with bypass instructions), (2) add `"prepare": "git config core.hooksPath .githooks 2>/dev/null || true"` to root `package.json`, so the hook auto-installs for every contributor on `pnpm install` / `npm install` / `yarn install` — no Husky dep, no extra setup step. Same pattern fits ECOSIRE.AI (Python validators on `backend/`), ECOSIRE.IO (deploy script gates), Development (Odoo manifest validators), OpenClaw (skill schema validators). Ship it on next pass.
- **Two re-confirmed gotchas worth re-flagging fleet-wide.** (a) `bash scripts/deploy-production.sh` again died at the PowerShell SSH stderr trap — Git Bash misreads ssh.exe stderr "[notice]" lines as PowerShell error-records; recovery is the now-routine `pnpm install → turbo build → pm2 restart → poll localhost:3000 → rm maintenance.flag → nginx -s reload` manual sequence. Same trap as 2026-04-19 + 2026-04-23 + this session. Worth elevating to a `do_ssh()` rewrite in deploy scripts (use `Out-Null` for stderr or wrap the bash invocation entirely outside PowerShell). (b) `translate-missing.mjs` re-translates whenever `existing[key] === enValue` so English-fallback rows DO get retranslated; `translate-single-locale.mjs` does NOT. Always use `translate-missing.mjs` after any `--fix` run.
- **Canonical facts promoted to Unity:** none (no new client/server/credential/price/module). Project-local memory `feedback_blog_i18n_keys_mandatory.md` rewritten to describe the new hook + the translator/Windows-lock gotchas. ECOSIRE.COM blog post count: 1,011 → **1,017 English** (× 11 locales = 11,187 MDX files).

- **Two reusable SSH-over-docker gotchas captured** — applies to any ECOSIRE workspace that shells into an ace-api-style container to run multi-line Python: (1) `ssh host "docker exec -c 'line1\nline2'"` collapses `\n` to literal backslash-n; fix is to base64-encode the script client-side and decode via `python -c 'import base64; exec(base64.b64decode("...").decode())'`. (2) Hardcoded prod host IPs in committed code fail the repo's pre-commit secret hook even when the value is already in committed CLAUDE.md; parameterize via env var (e.g. `ECOSIRE_PROD_SSH_TARGET`) with no default and look up the actual value from Unity's credentials inventory at runtime.
- Cross-project impact: auto-categorization ships to **every ECOSIRE.AI tenant** (not just freepcgames.org and pcgamestore.net) on next deploy — the 16-category taxonomy is shared canonical across the platform. Any other workspace that posts to WordPress through the strategy assistant will inherit the categorizer automatically. Base64-envelope SSH pattern is a reusable fleet-wide technique for running multi-line remote scripts safely. Saved locally as `feedback_wp_categories_auto_classify.md` + `project_category_classifier_2026_04_24.md` in ECOSIRE.AI project memory.

### 2026-04-24 — D:/ECOSIRE.COM — odovation.com outage + ecosire.com 3,700/day error cleanup (two deploys, zero data loss)
- **odovation `/services/[slug]` + `/integrations/[slug]` were 500 on every request** with redacted `digest: 'DYNAMIC_SERVER_USAGE'`. Root cause (reproducible locally only in prod build, not dev): `generateStaticParams` on these pages made Next.js 16 + Turbopack attempt static prerender, but `[locale]/layout.tsx` calls next-intl `getMessages()` without `setRequestLocale` — reads request-scoped context → throws at build → bundle ships broken. Removed `generateStaticParams` to match sibling muhammadamir. All 9 service slugs + 4 integration slugs now 200.
- **ecosire.com `/api/products/categories` 500×1,889/day** — Drizzle `select()` expanded column list the prod table couldn't satisfy (missing `organization_id` + `updated_at`) → Postgres 42703 silently swallowed by GlobalExceptionFilter. Fixed out-of-band with additive `ALTER TABLE ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS`, backfilled to real ECOSIRE org UUID. Extended same treatment to 6 more tables with leftover drift from the 2026-04-06 incident: `ga_page_snapshots.property_id`, `ga_aggregate_snapshots.property_id`, `gsc_query/country/device_snapshots.site_url`, `project_tasks` (+13 columns), `project_stages.rotting_threshold_days`. Scheduler crons now run clean.
- **~3,700 errors/day eliminated:** translator (Google Translate) had mangled ICU variable names inside `{...}` across 9 non-EN locales (`{industry}` → `{الصناعة}` / `{industrias}` / `{行业}` / `{名前}` / etc.) causing next-intl FORMATTING_ERROR at render. Built reusable `apps/web/scripts/fix-broken-icu-placeholders.mjs` (positional rewrite preserving translated surrounding text + ICU plural syntax) — fixed 160 strings. Also 16 Urdu blog posts had typo-truncated `</summar>` → `</summary>` crashing next-mdx-remote with "memory access out of bounds"; `fix-urdu-mdx-straggler-tags.mjs` handles these. Both scripts idempotent.
- Header CTA "Get Started" → "Sign up free" (English only, other 10 locales unchanged).
- Deploys: 1fa51b74 (odovation + categories + CTA) and 0368e5f9 (schema batch + placeholders + MDX). Both went via `/tmp/remote-deploy*.sh` through standard backup→maintenance→build→restart→health→maintenance-off sequence. Post-deploy smoke: AR/ZH/ES industries pages, Urdu blog posts, odovation services all 200. Past-3-min error log shows 0 FORMATTING_ERROR (was 1,830/day), 0 MDX RuntimeError (was 1,851/day). **Data floor: Products 215, Licenses 9, Leads 15, Contacts 3, Orders 0 — unchanged.**
- Cross-project impact: two reusable traps promoted to ECOSIRE project memory that ANY Next.js + next-intl project on this machine should avoid — `feedback_next_intl_static_params_trap.md` (never add `generateStaticParams` inside `[locale]/…/[slug]/page.tsx` if the layout calls `getMessages()`/`getTranslations()` without `setRequestLocale`; the failure mode is invisible — builds succeed, dev works, prod bundle 500s) and `feedback_translator_breaks_icu_placeholders.md` (always chain the placeholder-fixer script after ANY `translate-missing.mjs` run, or the translator silently breaks `{var}` references). Schema-drift repair pattern (upload .sh, `psql … -v ON_ERROR_STOP=1`, `ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS`, backfill org UUID, then `SET NOT NULL` + FK) is now a proven template for any Drizzle ORM workspace that takes a data-loss rollback. ### 2026-04-22 (late night) — D:/Development (Quicken Accounting / Wayfair) — v19.0.3.11.0 native Deduction/chargeback parsing shipped + prod payout rescued
- **Root bug:** `edi_parser.parse_payment_remittance` stopped at `Sub-total:` and let `Deduction,"PO#",date,…,amount` blocks leak into the invoice-line parser as phantom `chargeback` rows. Result: strict balance check failed (`expected_net − header_net` = sum of missing deductions ≠ 0), `_post_settlement_entries` rejected, payouts stuck in `imported`.
- **Fix shipped (v19.0.3.11.0):** new `_parse_deduction_blocks` helper emits one `adjustment` txn per chargeback with CreditID → `source_order_transaction_id` + Reason/Item/Memo/Desc → `note`; new Step 5b in `_post_settlement_entries` flips `reconciled=True, posting_status=posted` on every aggregate-booked fee/adjustment/chargeback line (fixes both `reconciliation_rate > 100%` AND deductions stuck showing "Pending" after post). Backported to v18 + v17 (pure-Python parser copied wholesale; surgical Edits elsewhere to avoid the `_sql_constraints` vs `models.Constraint` divergence).
- **Prod (soovah1) live:** module deployed via paramiko SFTP + `docker restart` (no `odoo -u` needed — pure Python patch). Payout 10002004859744 rescued from `imported` limbo: wiped 196 malformed rows, re-parsed to 185 sale + 11 adjustment, `_post_settlement_entries()` produced 188 JEs (185 per-invoice clearing payments + Fees $846.23 + Adjustments $964.27 + Wire $40,489.13). Backfill script retroactively marked aggregate lines reconciled on 3 already-posted payouts. **All 7 Quicken payouts now at 100.00% reconciliation, 0 pending aggregate lines.**
- **GitHub published (all 4 branches):** `ecosire/wayfair_store_management` @ main `b4bfed0` / 19.0 `1c24be8` / 18.0 `20f2c7c` / 17.0 `6b04294`. App Store HTML refreshed.
- **Two reusable fleet gotchas captured:** (1) `odoo -u` inside docker-compose fails with missing socket — pass `--db_host=db --db_port=5432 --db_user=... --db_password=...` explicitly, or just `docker restart` when patch is pure Python. (2) Scripts piped into `odoo shell` via stdin need explicit `from odoo import fields` — interactive shell globals don't propagate into `exec()`ed stdin body.
- Cross-project impact: both gotchas apply to EVERY docker-compose-deployed Odoo 19 tenant (Quicken / Diamond-STIG) and every odoo-shell repair script across the fleet. Saved as `feedback_code_restart_vs_module_update.md` + `feedback_odoo_shell_explicit_imports.md` in D:/Development project memory.
- Canonical facts promoted to Unity: [[Server & Key Inventory]] updated — Quicken row now flags `ecosire_main` as de-authorized (use password until re-appended) and lists Wayfair module @ v19.0.3.11.0.

### 2026-04-22 (evening) — D:/Development (Oenoteca production) — CSCS Inv 13972 booked + lot/serial tracking disabled fleet-wide
- **Bill booked + paid:** CSCS LLC Invoice #13972 → `BILL/2026/03/0013` dated 2026-03-18, $2,332.03 ($985 Freight 500002 + $1,347.03 Duty 500001) for PO P00114 Pierre Prieur et Fils (BL# 540600022902 Le Havre→Houston). Payment via manual JE `MISC/2026/03/0009` DR 211000 AP / CR 101401 Bank, reconciled → bill paid.
- **Lot/serial tracking disabled on 17 wine products** (all from Enohance shipment #77) after Nick confirmed he does not track lots/serials anywhere. `WH/OUT/00513` S00343 Uncorked/Altura Wine then validated (15 bottles shipped). 17 existing `stock.lot` rows + 12 lot-linked quants left in place; harmless with tracking=none.
- **Odoo 19 payment-flow gotcha (reusable for any Odoo 19 Enterprise client):** `account.payment.register` wizard can leave the payment in `state='in_process'` with `move_id=False` — the bill sticks at `payment_state='in_payment'`, residual unchanged, because the cash JE is never created. Root cause in Oenoteca's case: BNK1 outbound methods (Manual/Checks/NACHA) have `payment_account_id=False` (no Outstanding Payments account), and the client's actual workflow is direct bank-statement reconciliation without `account.payment` records (other paid bills have `matched_payment_ids=[]`). Fix that worked: delete the orphan payment + post a manual `account.move` (DR AP / CR Bank) + `account.move.line.reconcile` against the bill AP line. Worth checking for on any Odoo 19 Enterprise client using direct bank-recon.
- Cross-project impact: Odoo 19 payment pattern applies to every Odoo 19 Enterprise client in the fleet (Obliq, Sahara, Diamond/STIG, Alvi-Dental, Remittance).
- Canonical facts promoted to Unity: none (local Oenoteca inventory/AP state; no new client / server / credential).
